<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "--- Entry 0 ---\n[model] [PLAN MODE INSTRUCTIONS]\n\nYou are in PLAN MODE. You are architect. Your role is to analyze user requests and create structured task plans.\n\nMODE: PLAN ([--#THINKING#--ID1--])\n\nIMPORTANT WORKFLOW:\n\nPHASE 0 - CONTEXT GATHERING (MANDATORY):\nBefore creating ANY plan, you MUST understand the existing codebase:\n1. Call <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> to see project structure\n2. Call <ReadFile><fileName>README.md</fileName></ReadFile> to understand the project\n3. Call <ReadFile><fileName>AGENTS.md</fileName></ReadFile> to understand conventions\n4. List and read key config files (package.json, requirements.txt, config.py, etc.)\n5. Explore relevant directories with <List><path>src</path></List>\n\nDO NOT create a plan until you've gathered this context. The user may provide files to read directly.\n\nPHASE 1 - CREATE PLAN:\nCall <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal description</instructions></createPlan>\n\nPHASE 2 - CREATE TASKS:\nCall <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed instruction for this task</instruction></createTask> for each step\n\nPHASE 3 - FINALIZE:\nWhen all tasks are created, call <planDone/> to signal the plan is ready (this will ask if you want to switch to BUILD mode).\n\nHOW TO SPLIT USER INSTRUCTIONS INTO TASKS:\n1. Analyze the user's goal - what is the end result they want?\n2. Identify distinct steps that can be done independently\n3. Create tasks for each step with clear, actionable instructions\n4. Order matters - earlier tasks should enable later ones\n5. Be specific - each task should have a clear beginning and end\n\nTASK SIZE GUIDELINES (CRITICAL):\n- Each task should be completable in 1-5 minutes of AI work\n- A task represents ONE logical unit (e.g., \"Create login form\" not \"Build entire auth system\")\n- If a task requires >3 file edits, split it into smaller tasks\n- Tasks should be independently verifiable\n- Prefer 5-10 small tasks over 1-2 large ones\n- Each task should have clear success criteria\n\nWHY SPLIT INTO TASKS:\n- Easier to track progress\n- Can resume if interrupted\n- Better error handling (failure of one task doesn't affect others)\n- Parallel work possible in future\n\nESSENTIAL PLAN TOOLS (use these three for the core workflow):\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal and context</instructions></createPlan> - Create the plan FIRST\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed step-by-step instruction for the model to follow when executing this task</instruction></createTask> - Add tasks AFTER creating plan\n- <planDone/> - Signal planning is complete (triggers switch to BUILD mode)\n\nOTHER PLAN TOOLS:\n- <updateTask><id>taskId</id><status>pending|completed|blocked</status></updateTask> - Update task status\n- <deleteTask><id>taskId</id></deleteTask> - Remove a task\n- <clearAllTasks/> - Remove ALL tasks from the current plan\n- <cancelPlan/> - Cancel and delete the current plan entirely\n- <viewTask/> or <viewTask><id>taskId</id></viewTask> - View plan or specific task\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks in current plan\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> - Show directory tree. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\n\nTOOL USAGE GUIDELINES:\n(NOTE: The writing/editing tools below \u2014 Terminal, WriteFile, AppendFile, ReplaceLine, etc. \u2014 are BUILD-mode only. In PLAN mode they will be rejected. Use only plan tools listed above.)\n- Terminal: Use ONLY for one-liner commands. For complex scripts or data processing, use WriteFile/CreateFile.\n- WriteFile / CreateFile: Use for content < 2048 bytes in one call, or when creating a file from scratch.\n- AppendFile: Use when content > 2048 bytes (write first chunk with WriteFile, then AppendFile for rest). Also use for adding new content to existing files \u2014 avoids rewriting the whole file.\n- ReplaceLine: Use for targeted line edits. **TWO-STEP WORKFLOW:**\n  Step 1 \u2014 PREVIEW: Call **without** `<confirmed>`. The tool returns \"Line X currently reads: ... Proposed replacement: ...\" so you can verify your edit before applying.\n  Step 2 \u2014 CONFIRM: If the preview looks correct, call again WITH `<confirmed>true</confirmed>` to execute the replacement.\n  \n  This saves you a ReadFile call \u2014 the preview shows the old content. If it doesn't match what you expected (wrong line numbers, wrong text), adjust and preview again.\n\n  **CRITICAL ReplaceLine rules:**\n  - The parameter is <replacement>, NOT <content> or <contentOfFile>. WRONG: <content>Hello</content> -> ERROR. RIGHT: <replacement>Hello</replacement>\n  - Always ReadFile first to count lines and get exact line numbers (1-indexed)\n  - When replacing a block (CSS rule, function, class), include BOTH the opening AND closing delimiters in the range\n  - Example: to replace a block on lines 15-22, set fromLine=15, toLine=22\n  - After confirmed replacement, verify with ReadFile if the preview was truncated (showed \"...\" at the end)\n  - **Edge case \u2014 last block in file**: When editing the final block (e.g. `if __name__ == \"__main__\":`), include the block header in the `fromLine`..`toLine` range. If you replace only the indented body, the header is left orphaned. Example: to replace lines 26-29, use `fromLine=26`, `toLine=29`, and include all 4 lines in `<replacement>`.\n  - If unsure about line range, replace fewer lines and iterate\n  - Multi-line replacement: put raw newlines inside <replacement>...</replacement>. Replacing 1 line with N lines shifts later line numbers by N-1.\n\n  ReplaceLine examples:\n  Single line:\n  <ReplaceLine>\n    <fileName>config.py</fileName>\n    <fromLine>5</fromLine>\n    <replacement>DEBUG = True</replacement>\n  </ReplaceLine>\n\n  Multi-line block:\n  <ReplaceLine>\n    <fileName>app.py</fileName>\n    <fromLine>10</fromLine>\n    <toLine>12</toLine>\n    <replacement>def new_function():\n      print(\"new code\")\n      return 42</replacement>\n  </ReplaceLine>\n- TreeView: Use to explore project directory structure. Set depth=0 for unlimited depth.\n- General Rule: NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Grep / Find / List / TreeView: Prefer these XML tools over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n- EDITING MINDSET: Just as planning splits a big job into small focused tasks, split big file writes into small targeted edits. Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. Targeted edits are more precise, safer, and preserve previously written content.\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW:\n1. User says: \"I want a web app with login and dashboard\"\n2. You FIRST create the plan:\n   <createPlan><title>Web App Development</title><instructions>Create a web application with user authentication (login) and a dashboard for logged-in users.</instructions></createPlan>\n3. Then you create tasks:\n   <createTask><title>Setup Project Structure</title><instruction>Create project folder with basic files: index.html, style.css, app.js, server.py. Initialize npm if needed.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Create Backend API</title><instruction>Create server.py with Flask/FastAPI. Add login endpoint /api/login that validates username/password and returns JWT token. Add /api/dashboard endpoint that requires auth.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Build Frontend Login</title><instruction>Create index.html with login form. Connect to /api/login. Store JWT token in localStorage. Redirect to dashboard on success.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Build Dashboard</title><instruction>Create dashboard view. Fetch user data from /api/dashboard with token. Display user info and logout button.</instruction></createTask>\n\nWhen all tasks are created, call <planDone/> to signal the plan is ready and start building.\n\n[model] [BUILD MODE INSTRUCTIONS]\n\nYou are in BUILD MODE. You are code agent. Your role is to execute the tasks created in plan mode.\n\nMODE: BUILD ([--#THINKING#--ID1--])\n\nIMPORTANT WORKFLOW:\n1. You will receive tasks automatically (from plan mode). Execute each task using available tools.\n2. If you created your own tasks in build mode, call <planDone/> to start executing the first task.\n3. MANDATORY PROGRESS REPORTING: After completing any meaningful step, call <LogProgress><taskId>TASK_ID</taskId><whatWasDone>Specific action completed</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n4. MANDATORY SELF-VERIFICATION: Before calling <nextTask>completed</nextTask>, verify your work:\n   - If you wrote code: verify it runs or read it back with ReadFile\n   - If you made edits: verify changes with ReadFile\n   - If you created files: confirm they exist with List or TreeView\n   - If you deleted files: confirm they no longer exist\n5. When a task is verified completed, call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\n6. If blocked, call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> with detailed explanation\n7. When all tasks done, call <jobDone/> to finish the plan\n\nBLOCKED TASK HANDLING:\nWhen you encounter a blocker:\n1. <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "--- Entry 0 ---\n[model] [PLAN MODE INSTRUCTIONS]\n\nYou are in PLAN MODE. You are a literary architect \u2014 outline books, plan analysis, structure writing projects.\n\nMODE: PLAN ([--#THINKING#--ID1--])\n\nYOUR ROLE: Two modes of operation \u2014 book analysis or book writing.\n\nPHASE 0 - DISCOVERY:\nExplore the project working directory to find existing materials:\n1. <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> \u2014 find book files (.txt, .md, .pdf, .docx, .epub)\n2. <List><path>workout</path></List> \u2014 check for previous outputs\n3. Ask the user what they want: analyze an existing book or write a new one?\n\nPHASE 1 - UNDERSTAND THE GOAL:\n\n**For Analysis:**\n- Determine the book format (txt, pdf, docx, epub, md)\n- Note file size \u2014 decide how to read it (chunks if large)\n- Identify what analysis is wanted: structure? themes? characters? style?\n- Plan the output format (markdown report, JSON, scene breakdown, etc.)\n\n**For Writing:**\n- Discuss genre, target audience, tone, length\n- Outline the structure (parts, chapters, scenes)\n- Define characters, setting, themes upfront\n- Decide on file format for the manuscript (markdown recommended)\n\nPHASE 2 - CREATE STRUCTURED PLAN:\nCreate tasks with <createPlan> and <createTask>:\n\n**Analysis tasks example:**\n- Task 1: Read and summarize each chapter\n- Task 2: Identify characters and their arcs\n- Task 3: Map plot structure (three-act, hero's journey, etc.)\n- Task 4: Analyze themes and motifs\n- Task 5: Compile analysis report\n\n**Writing tasks example:**\n- Task 1: Create book outline (chapters, POV, timeline)\n- Task 2: Develop character profiles and setting bible\n- Task 3: Write Chapter 1\n- Task 4: Write Chapter 2\n- (one task per chapter, plus editing passes)\n\nPHASE 3 - FINALIZE:\nWhen all tasks are created, call <planDone/>.\n\nAVAILABLE PLAN TOOLS:\n- <createPlan> \u2014 start a plan\n- <createTask> \u2014 add tasks\n- <planDone/> \u2014 signal completion\n- <updateTask>, <deleteTask>, <viewTask>, <listTasks> \u2014 manage tasks\n\nIMPORTANT:\n- Save ALL analysis to workout/ or project files\n- For large books, read in chunks: <Head><fileName>book.txt</fileName><lines>100</lines></Head>\n- Save notes as tips with <SaveTip> so the model can reference them later\n\n[model] [BUILD MODE INSTRUCTIONS]\n\nYou are in BUILD MODE. You are a literary assistant \u2014 analyze books or help write them.\n\nMODE: BUILD ([--#THINKING#--ID1--])\n\nWORKFLOW:\n1. If working from a plan, execute tasks in order\n2. Track progress with <LogProgress>\n3. When a task is complete, verify with <ReadFile> then call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\n4. When all tasks are done, call <jobDone/>\n\n=== READING DIFFERENT FORMATS ===\n\n**TXT / MD \u2014 Plain text:**\n- Use <ReadFile><fileName>book.txt</fileName></ReadFile> (whole file) or <Head>/<Tail> for large files\n- For very long books, read in chunks: <Head><fileName>book.txt</fileName><lines>200</lines></Head> then <Tail>\n\n**PDF \u2014 Adobe PDF:**\n- Use <ReadPDF><fileName>book.pdf</fileName></ReadPDF>\n- Supports page ranges: <ReadPDF><fileName>book.pdf</fileName><fromPage>1</fromPage><toPage>20</toPage></ReadPDF>\n- Returns PDF metadata + text content per page\n\n**DOCX \u2014 Word documents:**\n- Use <Terminal><arg1>python3</arg1><arg2>-c</arg2><arg3>\nfrom docx import Document; doc = Document(\"book.docx\"); [print(p.text) for p in doc.paragraphs if p.text.strip()]\n</arg3></Terminal>\n\n**EPUB \u2014 E-books:**\n- Use <Terminal><arg1>python3</arg1><arg2>-c</arg2><arg3>\nfrom ebooklib import epub; from bs4 import BeautifulSoup; book = epub.read_epub(\"book.epub\")\nfor item in book.get_items():\n  if item.get_type() == 9:\n    soup = BeautifulSoup(item.get_body_content(), 'lxml'); print(soup.get_text())\n</arg3></Terminal>\n\n=== ANALYSIS WORKFLOW ===\n\n**Step 1: Read the book.**\n- Start with metadata (title, author, length)\n- Read chapter by chapter using the appropriate format reader\n- For long books, take notes as you go with <SaveTip>\n\n**Step 2: Analyze chapter by chapter.**\nFor each chapter, note:\n- Chapter summary (2-3 sentences)\n- Key events\n- Characters appearing\n- Notable quotes\nSave as structured notes.\n\n**Step 3: Structural analysis.**\n- Identify acts/parts and their purpose\n- Plot points (inciting incident, midpoint, climax, resolution)\n- Pacing analysis (fast/slow sections)\n- Chapter length distribution\n\n**Step 4: Character analysis.**\nFor each character:\n- Role in story (protagonist, antagonist, sidekick, foil)\n- Character arc (how do they change?)\n- Relationships with other characters\n- Dialogue style, notable traits\n\n**Step 5: Thematic analysis.**\n- Identify 3-5 major themes\n- Find supporting passages\n- Analyze how themes develop across the book\n\n**Step 6: Save analysis.**\nWrite the complete analysis to workout/analysis_report.md:\n<WriteFile><fileName>workout/analysis_report.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Analysis Report\n...\n</contentOfFile></WriteFile>\n\n=== WRITING WORKFLOW ===\n\n**Step 1: Create the foundation.**\nCreate a book bible (characters, setting, lore):\n<WriteFile><fileName>workout/book_bible.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Book Bible\n...\n</contentOfFile></WriteFile>\n\n**Step 2: Write chapter by chapter.**\nEach chapter gets its own file for clarity:\n- workout/chapter_01.md\n- workout/chapter_02.md\n- etc.\n\nUse <WriteFile> for new chapters, <AppendFile> to add sections to existing ones.\n\n**Step 3: Track progress.**\nMaintain a master outline as the table of contents:\n<WriteFile><fileName>workout/outline.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Outline\n- [x] Chapter 1: The Beginning\n- [ ] Chapter 2: The Journey\n...\n</contentOfFile></WriteFile>\nUpdate it as you complete chapters.\n\n**Step 4: Edit and revise.**\n- Create editing passes as separate tasks\n- Track word count with: <Terminal><arg1>wc</arg1><arg2>-w</arg2><arg3>workout/chapter_01.md</arg3></Terminal>\n- Use <ReplaceLine> for targeted edits on specific passages\n\n=== AVAILABLE TOOLS ===\n\nReading & Writing:\n- <ReadFile> \u2014 read plain text files\n- <ReadPDF> \u2014 read PDF books (with metadata + page extraction)\n- <WriteFile> \u2014 create new files\n- <AppendFile> \u2014 add to existing files\n- <ReplaceLine> \u2014 edit specific lines (use preview first with <confirmed>true</confirmed>)\n- <Head><lines>N</lines> \u2014 first N lines\n- <Tail><lines>N</lines> \u2014 last N lines\n\nFile Management:\n- <List> \u2014 list directory\n- <TreeView> \u2014 explore structure\n- <Find> \u2014 find files by pattern\n- <Grep> \u2014 search for text within files\n- <Terminal> \u2014 run # KosXER - X11 Configuration Editor
> 
> A Python/tkinter GUI application for editing Unix/Linux configuration files including `.Xresources`, OpenBox `menu.xml` and `rc.xml`, KosDWM configs, and other key-value configuration formats.
> 
> ## Features
> 
> - **Dual-pane layout**: File browser + tabbed editor
> - **Multiple format support**:
>   - `.Xresources` / `.Xdefaults` - X11 resource definitions with live apply
>   - `menu.xml` / `rc.xml` - OpenBox configuration
>   - KosDWM `config.json` and menu files
>   - Ge...

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "# KosXER - X11 Configuration Editor\n\nA Python/tkinter GUI application for editing Unix/Linux configuration files including `.Xresources`, OpenBox `menu.xml` and `rc.xml`, KosDWM configs, and other key-value configuration formats.\n\n## Features\n\n- **Dual-pane layout**: File browser + tabbed editor\n- **Multiple format support**:\n  - `.Xresources` / `.Xdefaults` - X11 resource definitions with live apply\n  - `menu.xml` / `rc.xml` - OpenBox configuration\n  - KosDWM `config.json` and menu files\n  - Generic key-value configs (`.conf`, `.env`, `.rc`, `.bashrc`, `.zshrc`)\n- **Intelligent Presets** - Auto-detects resource types and suggests colors, fonts, booleans\n- **Syntax-aware editing** with validation\n- **Live XResources Apply** - Click \"Apply\" to reload resources without restart\n- **XTerm Helper** - Launch new xterm with current resources + restart tips\n- **Show/Hide Hidden Files** - Toggle in file browser (Ctrl+H)\n- **Backup on save** - automatic `.bak` file creation\n- **Search and filter** capabilities\n- **Recent files** history\n- **Auto-versioning** - Version increments on every git commit\n\n## Installation\n\n```bash\n# Clone the repository\ngit clone https://github.com/m5it/kosxer.git\ncd kosxer\n\n# Install dependencies\npip install -r requirements.txt\n\n# Setup git hook for auto-versioning (optional)\nchmod +x .git/hooks/pre-commit\n\n# Run the application\npython main.py\n```\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n# Launch with default empty workspace\npython main.py\n\n# Open specific file\npython main.py ~/.Xresources\n\n# Open OpenBox menu\npython main.py ~/.config/openbox/menu.xml\n\n# Check version\npython AUTOVERSION.py --show\n```\n\n## Project Structure\n\n```\nKosXER/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 AUTOVERSION.py      # Single source of truth for version\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 config/             # Configuration settings\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 constants.py\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 presets.py      # Known values database\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 settings.py\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 VERSION\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 gui/                # UI components and widgets\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 editor_base.py\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 file_browser.py\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 xresources_editor.py\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 openbox_editor.py\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 kv_editor.py\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 kosdwm_config_editor.py\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 kosdwm_menu_editor.py\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 parsers/            # File format parsers\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 __init__.py\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 xresources_parser.py\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 openbox_parser.py\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 keyvalue_parser.py\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 kosdwm_parser.py\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 utils/              # Utility functions\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 backup.py\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 main.py             # Application entry point\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 requirements.txt    # Python dependencies\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 CHANGELOG.md        # Version history\n```\n\n## Supported File Formats\n\n| Format | Extension | Features |\n|--------|-----------|----------|\n| X Resources | `.Xresources`, `.Xdefaults` | Preprocessor directives, wildcards, colors, **Apply button**, **Intelligent Presets** |\n| OpenBox Menu | `menu.xml` | Nested menus, actions, icons |\n| OpenBox RC | `rc.xml` | Keybindings, themes, settings |\n| KosDWM Config | `config.json` | JSON-based DWM configuration |\n| KosDWM Menu | `menu.json` | Application menu definitions |\n| Generic Config | `.conf`, `.rc`, `.env` | Sections, key-value pairs, shell exports |\n\n## Keyboard Shortcuts\n\n| Shortcut | Action |\n|----------|--------|\n| `Ctrl+O` | Open file |\n| `Ctrl+S` | Save |\n| `Ctrl+Shift+S` | Save as |\n| `Ctrl+W` | Close tab |\n| `Ctrl+Q` | Quit |\n| `Ctrl+B` | Toggle file browser |\n| `Ctrl+H` | Toggle hidden files |\n| `F5` | Refresh file browser |\n| `Ctrl+Z` | Undo |\n| `Ctrl+Y` | Redo |\n\n## Intelligent Presets\n\nKosXER automatically detects resource types and suggests appropriate values:\n\n### How It Works\n\nWhen you double-click a resource to edit, KosXER analyzes the resource name:\n\n| Resource Pattern | Detected Type | Editor Shown |\n|------------------|---------------|--------------|\n| `*color*`, `*background`, `*foreground` | Color | Color picker + preset palette |\n| `*font*`, `*face*` | Font | Font dropdown with presets |\n| `*scroll*`, `*bell*`, `*bold*` | Boolean | True/False dropdown |\n| Others | Generic | Text editor with preset picker |\n\n### Using Presets\n\n1. **Double-click** any resource to edit\n2. For colors: See color picker + quick presets (White, Black, Red, etc.)\n3. For fonts: Choose from common monospace fonts\n4. For booleans: Select true/false/yes/no/on/off\n5. Or use **\"Insert Preset\"** button for full preset browser\n\n### Preset Categories\n\n- **Colors** \ud83c\udfa8 - 16 terminal colors + common colors\n- **Fonts** \ud83d\udd24 - xft fonts (Monospace, DejaVu, Source Code Pro, etc.)\n- **Booleans** \u2611\ufe0f - true/false, yes/no, on/off, 1/0\n- **XTerm** \ud83d\udcbb - Common xterm resource values\n\n## XResources Live Apply\n\nEdit your `.Xresources` and apply changes **without logging out**:\n\n1. Open `~/.Xresources`\n2. Edit colors or values\n3. **Save** (Ctrl+S)\n4. Click **\"Apply (xrdb)\"** button\n5. Changes take effect immediately!\n\nThe Apply button runs `xrdb -merge ~/.Xresources` and shows success/error messages.\n\n## XTerm Color Reference\n\nStandard terminal color palette (color0-color15):\n\n| Color | Hex Value | Usage |\n|-------|-----------|-------|\n| color0 | `#000000` | Black |\n| color1 | `#ff0000` | Red |\n| color2 | `#00ff00` | Green |\n| color3 | `#ffff00` | Yellow |\n| color4 | `#0000ff` | Blue |\n| color5 | `#ff00ff` | Magenta |\n| color6 | `#00ffff` | Cyan |\n| **color7** | **`#ffffff`** | **White** |\n| color8 | `#808080` | Bright Black |\n| color9 | `#ff5555` | Bright Red |\n| color10 | `#55ff55` | Bright Green |\n| color11 | `#ffff55` | Bright Yellow |\n| color12 | `#5555ff` | Bright Blue |\n| color13 | `#ff55ff` | Bright Magenta |\n| color14 | `#55ffff` | Bright Cyan |\n| **color15** | **`#ffffff`** | **Bright White** |\n\n### Common XTerm White Background Examples\n\n```bash\n# Pure white background with black text\nXTerm*background: #ffffff\nXTerm*foreground: #000000\n\n# Off-white background\nXTerm*background: #f0f0f0\nXTerm*foreground: #000000\n\n# Using color7 (white)\nXTerm*background: color7\nXTerm*foreground: color0\n```\n\n## XTerm Helper\n\nKosXER includes special buttons to help with xterm:\n\n- **\"New XTerm\"** - Launches fresh xterm with current resources applied\n- **\"XTerm Tips\"** - Shows help dialog explaining restart behavior\n\n### Why xterm Needs Restart\n\n**Important:** `xrdb -merge` only affects **NEW** xterm windows!\n\n- Running xterm instances keep their old resources\n- Changes only appear in windows opened AFTER applying\n- Use **\"New XTerm\"** button to see changes immediately\n\n## Auto-Versioning\n\nKosXER uses `AUTOVERSION.py` as the single source of truth:\n\n- Version is defined once in `AUTOVERSION.py`\n- Git pre-commit hook auto-increments version (1.0.0 \u2192 1.0.1)\n- Version displayed in window title and About dialog\n- Import anywhere: `from AUTOVERSION import VERSION`\n\n```bash\n# Check current version\npython AUTOVERSION.py --show\n\n# Manual version bump\npython AUTOVERSION.py\n```\n\n## File Browser Features\n\n- **Quick Access** panel for common config locations\n- **Show/Hide Hidden Files** toggle (checkbox + Ctrl+H)\n- **File System** tree view with navigation\n- **Filter** by file type (only shows supported configs)\n- Double-click to open files\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Changes Don't Appear in xterm\n\n**Problem:** Applied resources but xterm looks the same\n\n**Solution:**\n1. Click **\"New XTerm\"** button to launch fresh window\n2. Or close all xterm windows and reopen them\n3. Remember: `xrdb -merge` only affects NEW windows\n\n### xrdb Command Not Found\n\n**Problem:** \"xrdb not found\" error when applying\n\n**Solution:**\n```bash\n# Install x11-xserver-utils (contains xrdb)\nsudo apt-get install x11-xserver-utils   # Debian/Ubuntu\nsudo yum install xorg-x11-xutils         # RHEL/CentOS\n```\n\n### White Background Not Working\n\n**Problem:** Set white background but xterm still dark\n\n**Solution:**\n```bash\n# Check if resource is being overridden\nxrdb -query | grep -i background\n\n# Use specific resource path\necho \"XTerm*background: #ffffff\" | xrdb -merge\n```\n\n## Development\n\n```bash\n# Run tests\npython -m pytest parsers/\n\n# Test specific parser\npython parsers/test_xresources.py\npython parsers/test_openbox.py\npython parsers/test_keyvalue.py\n\n# Check code style\nflake8 parsers/ gui/ --max-line-length=100\n```\n\n## Requirements\n\n- Python 3.8+\n- tkinter (usually included with Python)\n- watchdog (optional, for file watching)\n- lxml (for XML parsing)\n\n```bash\npip install -r requirements.txt\n```\n\n## License\n\nMIT License - See LICENSE file for details.\n\n## Contributing\n\nContributions welcome! Please submit pull requests or open issues for bugs and feature requests.\n\n### Feature Ideas\n\n- [ ] Syntax highlighting in editors\n- [ ] Live preview for colors\n- [ ] Import/export themes\n- [ ] Plugin system for custom parsers\n- [ ] Dark/light theme toggle\n\n---\n\n**Current Version:** Import from `AUTOVERSION.py`\n", "sessionId": 327, "rowId": 0, "timestamp": 1784289997.2284894, "date": "2026-07-17", "name": "ReadFile"} -->

#!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> Main Window for KosXER

#!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> Base Editor Widget for KosXER
> 
> Abstract base class for all editor widgets. Provides common functionality
> including toolbar, status area, change tracking, and file operations.

>     Abstract base class for all editor widgets.

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nBase Editor Widget for KosXER\n\nAbstract base class for all editor widgets. Provides common functionality\nincluding toolbar, status area, change tracking, and file operations.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk, messagebox\nfrom abc import ABC, abstractmethod\nfrom typing import Optional, Callable, Any, Dict\n\n\nclass EditorWidget(ABC, ttk.Frame):\n    \"\"\"\n    Abstract base class for all editor widgets.\n    \n    Subclasses must implement:\n    - _create_editor_widgets(): Create the specific editor UI\n    - load_data(data): Load data into the editor\n    - get_data(): Get data from the editor\n    - validate(): Validate the current data\n    \n    Features:\n    - Common toolbar with Save, Reload, Validate buttons\n    - Status area for messages\n    - Change tracking (dirty flag)\n    - Integration with main window for file operations\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, parent, main_window=None, filepath: Optional[str] = None, \n                 *args, **kwargs):\n        \"\"\"\n        Initialize the editor widget.\n        \n        Args:\n            parent: Parent widget\n            main_window: Reference to main window for callbacks\n            filepath: Path to the file being edited\n        \"\"\"\n        super().__init__(parent, *args, **kwargs)\n        \n        self.main_window = main_window\n        self.filepath = filepath\n        self._dirty = False\n        self._data: Any = None\n        self._original_data: Any = None\n        \n        # Callbacks\n        self._on_save_callback: Optional[Callable] = None\n        self._on_change_callback: Optional[Callable] = None\n        \n        # Create UI\n        self._create_toolbar()\n        self._create_editor_area()\n        self._create_statusbar()\n        \n        # Layout\n        self.toolbar.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=5, pady=2)\n        self.editor_frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)\n        self.statusbar.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=5, pady=2)\n    \n    def _create_toolbar(self):\n        \"\"\"Create the common toolbar.\"\"\"\n        self.toolbar = ttk.Frame(self)\n        \n        # Save button\n        self.save_btn = ttk.Button(\n            self.toolbar, \n            text=\"\ud83d\udcbe Save\", \n            command=self._on_save,\n            state=tk.DISABLED\n        )\n        self.save_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=2)\n        \n        # Reload button\n        self.reload_btn = ttk.Button(\n            self.toolbar,\n            text=\"\ud83d\udd04 Reload\",\n            command=self._on_reload\n        )\n        self.reload_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=2)\n        \n        # Validate button\n        self.validate_btn = ttk.Button(\n            self.toolbar,\n            text=\"\u2713 Validate\",\n            command=self._on_validate\n        )\n        self.validate_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=2)\n        \n        ttk.Separator(self.toolbar, orient=tk.VERTICAL).pack(\n            side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.Y, padx=10\n        )\n        \n        # File info label\n        self.file_label = ttk.Label(self.toolbar, text=\"No file\")\n        self.file_label.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Dirty indicator\n        self.dirty_indicator = ttk.Label(\n            self.toolbar, \n            text=\"\",\n            foreground=\"red\",\n            font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')\n        )\n        self.dirty_indicator.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)\n    \n    def _create_editor_area(self):\n        \"\"\"Create the main editor area. Subclasses implement actual editor.\"\"\"\n        self.editor_frame = ttk.Frame(self, relief=tk.SUNKEN, borderwidth=1)\n        \n        # This will be filled by subclass _create_editor_widgets()\n        self._create_editor_widgets()\n    \n    def _create_statusbar(self):\n        \"\"\"Create the status bar.\"\"\"\n        self.statusbar = ttk.Frame(self, relief=tk.SUNKEN, borderwidth=1)\n        \n        self.status_label = ttk.Label(\n            self.statusbar,\n            text=\"Ready\",\n            anchor=tk.W\n        )\n        self.status_label.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True, padx=5)\n        \n        self.position_label = ttk.Label(\n            self.statusbar,\n            text=\"\",\n            anchor=tk.E\n        )\n        self.position_label.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)\n    \n    @abstractmethod\n    def _create_editor_widgets(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Create editor-specific widgets.\n        \n        Must be implemented by subclasses to create their specific UI\n        within self.editor_frame.\n        \"\"\"\n        pass\n    \n    # Required abstract methods\n    \n    @abstractmethod\n    def load_data(self, data: Any):\n        \"\"\"\n        Load data into the editor.\n        \n        Args:\n            data: Data to load (format depends on parser)\n        \"\"\"\n        pass\n    \n    @abstractmethod\n    def get_data(self) -> Any:\n        \"\"\"\n        Get current data from the editor.\n        \n        Returns:\n            Current editor data\n        \"\"\"\n        pass\n    \n    @abstractmethod\n    def validate(self) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Validate the current data.\n        \n        Returns:\n            Tuple of (is_valid, error_message)\n        \"\"\"\n        pass\n    \n    # Common methods\n    \n    def has_changes(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if editor has unsaved changes.\"\"\"\n        return self._dirty\n    \n    def mark_dirty(self, dirty: bool = True):\n        \"\"\"\n        Mark the editor as dirty (has changes).\n        \n        Args:\n            dirty: True if has changes, False if clean\n        \"\"\"\n        self._dirty = dirty\n        \n        # Update UI\n        if dirty:\n            self.dirty_indicator.config(text=\"\u25cf Modified\")\n            self.save_btn.config(state=tk.NORMAL)\n        else:\n            self.dirty_indicator.config(text=\"\")\n            self.save_btn.config(state=tk.DISABLED)\n        \n        # Notify callback\n        if self._on_change_callback:\n            self._on_change_callback(dirty)\n    \n    def set_filepath(self, filepath: str):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set the file path being edited.\n        \n        Args:\n            filepath: Path to file\n        \"\"\"\n        self.filepath = filepath\n        display_path = filepath if len(filepath) < 50 else \"...\" + filepath[-47:]\n        self.file_label.config(text=display_path)\n    \n    def set_status(self, message: str, message_type: str = \"info\"):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set status bar message.\n        \n        Args:\n            message: Message to display\n            message_type: 'info', 'warning', or 'error'\n        \"\"\"\n        colors = {\n            \"info\": \"black\",\n            \"warning\": \"orange\",\n            \"error\": \"red\"\n        }\n        self.status_label.config(\n            text=message,\n            foreground=colors.get(message_type, \"black\")\n        )\n    \n    def set_position(self, position: str):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set position indicator (e.g., line/column).\n        \n        Args:\n            position: Position string to display\n        \"\"\"\n        self.position_label.config(text=position)\n    \n    def set_on_save_callback(self, callback: Callable):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set callback for save operation.\n        \n        Args:\n            callback: Function to call on save\n        \"\"\"\n        self._on_save_callback = callback\n    \n    def set_on_change_callback(self, callback: Callable[[bool], None]):\n        \"\"\"\n        Set callback for change events.\n        \n        Args:\n            callback: Function(bool) called when dirty state changes\n        \"\"\"\n        self._on_change_callback = callback\n    \n    def _on_save(self):\n        \"\"\"Handle save button click.\"\"\"\n        # Validate first\n        is_valid, error = self.validate()\n        if not is_valid:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Validation Error\", error)\n            self.set_status(f\"Validation failed: {error}\", \"error\")\n            return\n        \n        # Get current data\n        data = self.get_data()\n        \n        # Call save callback if set\n        if self._on_save_callback:\n            try:\n                self._on_save_callback(data)\n                self._original_data = data\n                self.mark_dirty(False)\n                self.set_status(\"Saved successfully\", \"info\")\n            except Exception as e:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Save Error\", str(e))\n                self.set_status(f\"Save failed: {str(e)}\", \"error\")\n        elif self.main_window:\n            # Use main window's save method\n            self.main_window.file_save()\n    \n    def _on_reload(self):\n        \"\"\"Handle reload button click.\"\"\"\n        if self.has_changes():\n            response = messagebox.askyesnocancel(\n                \"Unsaved Changes\",\n                \"You have unsaved changes. Save before reloading?\"\n            )\n            if response is True:\n                self._on_save()\n                if self.has_changes():  # Still dirty, save failed\n                    return\n            elif response is False:\n                pass  # Discard changes\n            else:  # Cancel\n                return\n        \n        # Reload original data\n        if self._original_data is not None:\n            self.load_data(self._original_data)\n            self.mark_dirty(False)\n            self.set_status(\"Reloaded from disk\", \"info\")\n    \n    def _on_validate(self):\n        \"\"\"Handle validate button click.\"\"\"\n        is_valid, error = self.validate()\n        if is_valid:\n            self.set_status(\"\u2713 Validation passed\", \"info\")\n            messagebox.showinfo(\"Validation\", \"Content is valid!\")\n        else:\n            self.set_status(f\"\u2717 Validation failed: {error}\", \"error\")\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Validation Error\", error)\n    \n    def reset(self):\n        \"\"\"Reset editor to empty state.\"\"\"\n        self._dirty = False\n        self._data = None\n        self._original_data = None\n        self.mark_dirty(False)\n        self.set_status(\"Ready\")\n    \n    def get_filepath(self) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Get current file path.\"\"\"\n        return self.filepath\n    \n    def is_dirty(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Alias for has_changes().\"\"\"\n        return self._dirty\n\n\nclass TextEditorWidget(EditorWidget):\n    \"\"\"\n    Example concrete implementation using a text widget.\n    Can be used for simple text-based configs.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def _create_editor_widgets(self):\n        \"\"\"Create text editor widgets.\"\"\"\n        # Text widget with scrollbars\n        text_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        text_frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)\n        \n        self.text_widget = tk.Text(\n            text_frame,\n            wrap=tk.NONE,\n            undo=True,\n            maxundo=50\n        )\n        \n        # Scrollbars\n        y_scrollbar = ttk.Scrollbar(text_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL)\n        x_scrollbar = ttk.Scrollbar(self.editor_frame, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL)\n        \n        self.text_widget.config(yscrollcommand=y_scrollbar.set,\n                               xscrollcommand=x_scrollbar.set)\n        y_scrollbar.config(command=self.text_widget.yview)\n        x_scrollbar.config(command=self.text_widget.xview)\n        \n        # Layout\n        y_scrollbar.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)\n        self.text_widget.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)\n        x_scrollbar.pack(fill=tk.X)\n        \n        # Bind change events\n        self.text_widget.bind(\"<<Modified>>\", self._on_text_modified)\n        self.text_widget.bind(\"<KeyRelease>\", self._on_cursor_move)\n        self.text_widget.bind(\"<ButtonRelease>\", self._on_cursor_move)\n    \n    def _on_text_modified(self, event=None):\n        \"\"\"Handle text modification.\"\"\"\n        if self.text_widget.edit_modified():\n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self.text_widget.edit_modified(False)\n    \n    def _on_cursor_move(self, event=None):\n        \"\"\"Update position indicator.\"\"\"\n        index = self.text_widget.index(tk.INSERT)\n        line, col = index.split('.')\n        self.set_position(f\"Line {line}, Col {col}\")\n    \n    def load_data(self, data: str):\n        \"\"\"Load text data.\"\"\"\n        self.text_widget.delete('1.0', tk.END)\n        self.text_widget.insert('1.0', data)\n        self._original_data = data\n        self.mark_dirty(False)\n    \n    def get_data(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get text data.\"\"\"\n        return self.text_widget.get('1.0', tk.END + '-1c')\n    \n    def validate(self) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n        \"\"\"Validate text content.\"\"\"\n        content = self.get_data()\n        if not content.strip():\n            return False, \"Content is empty\"\n        return True, \"\"\n", "sessionId": 327, "rowId": 0, "timestamp": 1784289997.2288215, "date": "2026-07-17", "name": "ReadFile"} -->

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nXResources Editor Widget for KosXER\n\nTreeview-based editor for .Xresources and .Xdefaults files.\nIncludes Apply button to reload resources with xrdb, preset picker, and user presets.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk, colorchooser, messagebox, simpledialog\nimport re\nimport subprocess\nimport os\nfrom typing import Optional, List\n\nfrom gui.editor_base import EditorWidget\nfrom parsers.xresources_parser import XResourcesParser, XResourceEntry\nfrom config.presets import (\n    get_presets_for_resource, get_all_presets, XTERM_COLORS,\n    add_user_preset, delete_user_preset, get_user_presets_list,\n    load_user_presets, USER_PRESETS_FILE\n)\n\n\nclass XResourcesEditor(EditorWidget):\n    \"\"\"Editor widget for XResources files.\"\"\"\n    \n    COLOR_HEX_PATTERN = re.compile(r'^#[0-9a-fA-F]{6}$')\n    COLOR_RGB_PATTERN = re.compile(r'^rgb:([0-9a-fA-F]{2,4})/([0-9a-fA-F]{2,4})/([0-9a-fA-F]{2,4})$')\n    \n    def __init__(self, parent, main_window=None, filepath: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs):\n        self.parser = XResourcesParser()\n        self.entries: List[XResourceEntry] = []\n        self.filtered_entries: List[XResourceEntry] = []\n        super().__init__(parent, main_window, filepath, **kwargs)\n    \n    def _create_editor_widgets(self):\n        \"\"\"Create the XResources editor UI.\"\"\"\n        # Filter frame\n        filter_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        filter_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        ttk.Label(filter_frame, text=\"Filter:\").pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        self.filter_var = tk.StringVar()\n        self.filter_var.trace('w', self._on_filter_changed)\n        ttk.Entry(filter_frame, textvariable=self.filter_var, width=30).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(filter_frame, text=\"Clear\", command=self._clear_filter).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Treeview\n        tree_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        tree_frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, pady=5)\n        \n        columns = ('resource', 'value', 'type', 'preview')\n        self.tree = ttk.Treeview(tree_frame, columns=columns, show='headings')\n        \n        self.tree.heading('resource', text='Resource Path')\n        self.tree.heading('value', text='Value')\n        self.tree.heading('type', text='Type')\n        self.tree.heading('preview', text='Preview')\n        \n        self.tree.column('resource', width=300)\n        self.tree.column('value', width=250)\n        self.tree.column('type', width=100)\n        self.tree.column('preview', width=50)\n        \n        y_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.tree.yview)\n        x_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.tree.xview)\n        self.tree.configure(yscrollcommand=y_scroll.set, xscrollcommand=x_scroll.set)\n        \n        y_scroll.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)\n        x_scroll.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)\n        self.tree.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)\n        \n        # Buttons\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Add Resource\", command=self._add_resource).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Delete Selected\", command=self._delete_selected).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Insert Preset\", command=self._show_preset_picker).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # User presets button\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"My Presets\", command=self._manage_user_presets).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # XTerm helper buttons\n        ttk.Separator(btn_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL).pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.Y, padx=10)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"New XTerm\", command=self._launch_new_xterm).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"XTerm Tips\", command=self._show_xterm_tips).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Apply button (reloads X resources)\n        self.apply_btn = ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Apply (xrdb)\", command=self._apply_resources, \n                                    state=tk.DISABLED)\n        self.apply_btn.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Info label about xterm restart\n        info_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        info_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=5, pady=2)\n        self.info_label = ttk.Label(info_frame, text=\"\ud83d\udca1 Tip: xterm needs restart to see changes. Use 'New XTerm' or close/reopen.\", \n                                   foreground=\"gray\", font=('Helvetica', 9, 'italic'))\n        self.info_label.pack(side=tk.LEFT)\n        \n        # Bindings\n        self.tree.bind('<Double-1>', self._on_double_click)\n    \n    def _detect_resource_type(self, resource_path: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Detect resource type from resource path name for intelligent suggestions.\n        \n        Args:\n            resource_path: Resource path like 'XTerm*background', '*.color0'\n        \n        Returns:\n            'color', 'font', 'boolean', 'number', or 'generic'\n        \"\"\"\n        if not resource_path:\n            return 'generic'\n        \n        path_lower = resource_path.lower()\n        \n        # Color patterns\n        color_patterns = ['color', 'background', 'foreground', 'cursorcolor', \n                       'bordercolor', 'highlightcolor', 'troughcolor']\n        if any(p in path_lower for p in color_patterns):\n            return 'color'\n        \n        # Font patterns\n        font_patterns = ['font', 'face', 'facename']\n        if any(p in path_lower for p in font_patterns):\n            return 'font'\n        \n        # Boolean patterns\n        bool_patterns = ['shell', 'video', 'scroll', 'bell', 'bold', 'allow', \n                        'blink', 'underline', 'active', 'enabled', 'visible',\n                        'reverse', 'iconic', 'hold', 'utmp']\n        if any(p in path_lower for p in bool_patterns):\n            return 'boolean'\n        \n        # Number patterns\n        num_patterns = ['lines', 'chars', 'pixels', 'width', 'height', 'size',\n                       'borderwidth', 'margin', 'padding', 'timeout', 'interval']\n        if any(p in path_lower for p in num_patterns):\n            return 'number'\n        \n        return 'generic'\n    \n    def _launch_new_xterm(self):\n        \"\"\"Launch a new xterm instance with current XResources.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            # First apply current resources\n            if self.filepath and os.path.exists(self.filepath):\n                subprocess.run(['xrdb', '-merge', self.filepath], check=True, capture_output=True)\n            \n            # Launch xterm in background\n            subprocess.Popen(['xterm'], stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL, stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL)\n            self.set_status(\"\u2713 Launched new xterm with current resources\")\n            \n        except FileNotFoundError:\n            # Try uxterm as fallback\n            try:\n                subprocess.Popen(['uxterm'], stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL, stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL)\n                self.set_status(\"\u2713 Launched new uxterm with current resources\")\n            except FileNotFoundError:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"xterm Not Found\", \n                                   \"Neither 'xterm' nor 'uxterm' found.\\n\\n\"\n                                   \"Install xterm: sudo apt-get install xterm\")\n        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Failed to apply resources: {e}\")\n    \n    def _show_xterm_tips(self):\n        \"\"\"Show dialog explaining xterm restart behavior.\"\"\"\n        tips_text = \"\"\"XTerm Resource Loading - How It Works\n\nWhy don't my changes appear immediately?\n\n1. xrdb -merge loads resources into the X server\n2. Running xterm instances keep their OLD resources\n3. Only NEW xterm windows see the changes\n\nSolutions:\n\n\u2713 Use \"New XTerm\" button\n  - Applies resources then launches fresh xterm\n  - New window sees all changes immediately\n\n\u2713 Close and reopen xterm\n  - Old window keeps old colors/fonts\n  - New window loads fresh resources\n\n\u2713 Start xterm with specific file\n  - xterm -xrm \"*background: #ffffff\"\n\nCommon White Colors for xterm:\n\n  XTerm*background: #ffffff    (pure white)\n  XTerm*foreground: #000000    (black text)\n  XTerm*background: #f0f0f0    (off-white)\n  XTerm*foreground: #ffffff    (white text)\n\nRemember: Save \u2192 Apply \u2192 New XTerm to see changes!\"\"\"\n        \n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"XTerm Tips\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.geometry(\"500x450\")\n        \n        text = tk.Text(dialog, wrap=tk.WORD, padx=10, pady=10, font=('Courier', 10))\n        text.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)\n        text.insert('1.0', tips_text)\n        text.config(state=tk.DISABLED)\n        \n        ttk.Button(dialog, text=\"Close\", command=dialog.destroy).pack(pady=5)\n    \n    def _get_value_type(self, value: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Determine value type from value string.\"\"\"\n        value = value.strip().lower()\n        \n        if self.COLOR_HEX_PATTERN.match(value) or self.COLOR_RGB_PATTERN.match(value):\n            return 'color'\n        if value in ['true', 'false', 'yes', 'no', 'on', 'off']:\n            return 'boolean'\n        if 'font' in value or value.startswith('xft:') or value.startswith('-*-'):\n            return 'font'\n        \n        try:\n            int(value)\n            return 'number'\n        except ValueError:\n            try:\n                float(value)\n                return 'number'\n            except ValueError:\n                pass\n        \n        return 'string'\n    \n    def _get_color_preview(self, value: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get color for preview.\"\"\"\n        if self.COLOR_HEX_PATTERN.match(value):\n            return value\n        return ''\n    \n    def _populate_tree(self):\n        \"\"\"Populate treeview with entries.\"\"\"\n        # Clear existing\n        for item in self.tree.get_children():\n            self.tree.delete(item)\n        \n        # Add filtered entries\n        for entry in self.filtered_entries:\n            value_type = self._get_value_type(entry.value)\n            preview = self._get_color_preview(entry.value) if value_type == 'color' else ''\n            \n            item_id = self.tree.insert('', 'end', values=(\n                entry.resource_path,\n                entry.value,\n                value_type,\n                preview\n            ))\n            \n            # Set tag for color background\n            if preview:\n                self.tree.item(item_id, tags=(preview,))\n                self.tree.tag_configure(preview, background=preview)\n    \n    def _on_filter_changed(self, *args):\n        \"\"\"Apply filter.\"\"\"\n        filter_text = self.filter_var.get().lower()\n        \n        if not filter_text:\n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        else:\n            self.filtered_entries = [\n                e for e in self.entries \n                if filter_text in e.resource_path.lower() or filter_text in e.value.lower()\n            ]\n        \n        self._populate_tree()\n    \n    def _clear_filter(self):\n        \"\"\"Clear filter.\"\"\"\n        self.filter_var.set('')\n        self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        self._populate_tree()\n    \n    def _on_double_click(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Handle double click for editing with intelligent type detection.\"\"\"\n        selection = self.tree.selection()\n        if not selection:\n            return\n        \n        item = selection[0]\n        values = self.tree.item(item, 'values')\n        if not values:\n            return\n        \n        resource_path, current_value, value_type, _ = values\n        \n        # Use intelligent detection based on resource name\n        detected_type = self._detect_resource_type(resource_path)\n        \n        # Override with detected type if it's more specific\n        if detected_type == 'color' or value_type == 'color':\n            self._edit_color_with_presets(resource_path, current_value)\n        elif detected_type == 'font':\n            self._edit_with_presets(resource_path, current_value, 'font')\n        elif detected_type == 'boolean':\n            self._edit_with_presets(resource_path, current_value, 'boolean')\n        else:\n            self._edit_generic(resource_path, current_value)\n    \n    def _edit_color_with_presets(self, resource_path: str, current_value: str):\n        \"\"\"Edit color with color picker and preset colors.\"\"\"\n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(f\"Edit Color - {resource_path}\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        dialog.geometry(\"400x550\")\n        \n        # Current value display\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Current Value:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=5)\n        current_var = tk.StringVar(value=current_value)\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=current_var, width=40, state='readonly').pack(padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        # Color preview\n        preview_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog, width=100, height=50)\n        preview_frame.pack(pady=10)\n        preview_frame.pack_propagate(False)\n        \n        preview_label = tk.Label(preview_frame, text=\"Preview\", bg=current_value if self.COLOR_HEX_PATTERN.match(current_value) else 'gray')\n        preview_label.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)\n        \n        # Color picker button\n        def pick_color():\n            initial = current_var.get()\n            if self.COLOR_RGB_PATTERN.match(initial):\n                match = self.COLOR_RGB_PATTERN.match(initial)\n                if match:\n                    r, g, b = match.groups()\n                    initial = f\"#{r[:2]}{g[:2]}{b[:2]}\"\n            \n            color = colorchooser.askcolor(initialcolor=initial, title=\"Choose Color\")\n            if color and color[1]:\n                current_var.set(color[1])\n                preview_label.config(bg=color[1])\n        \n        ttk.Button(dialog, text=\"\ud83c\udfa8 Pick Color...\", command=pick_color).pack(pady=5)\n        \n        # Preset colors\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Quick Presets:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=5)\n        \n        preset_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        preset_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        # Show common colors in a grid\n        common_colors = [\n            ('White', '#ffffff'), ('Black', '#000000'),\n            ('Red', '#ff0000'), ('Green', '#00ff00'),\n            ('Blue', '#0000ff'), ('Yellow', '#ffff00'),\n            ('Cyan', '#00ffff'), ('Magenta', '#ff00ff'),\n            ('Gray', '#808080'), ('Orange', '#ffa500'),\n        ]\n        \n        for i, (name, color) in enumerate(common_colors):\n            btn = tk.Button(preset_frame, text=name, bg=color, fg='white' if color in ['#000000', '#0000ff', '#808080'] else 'black',\n                          width=8, command=lambda c=color: (current_var.set(c), preview_label.config(bg=c)))\n            btn.grid(row=i//5, column=i%5, padx=2, pady=2)\n        \n        # Terminal colors\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Terminal Colors:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=5)\n        \n        term_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        term_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        for i in range(8):\n            color_val = XTERM_COLORS[f'color{i}']\n            btn = tk.Button(term_frame, text=f\"color{i}\", bg=color_val, \n                          fg='white' if i in [0, 4] else 'black',\n                          width=8, command=lambda c=color_val: (current_var.set(c), preview_label.config(bg=c)))\n            btn.grid(row=0, column=i, padx=2, pady=2)\n        \n        # Save as preset button\n        def save_as_preset():\n            name = simpledialog.askstring(\"Save Preset\", \"Enter preset name:\", parent=dialog)\n            if name:\n                if add_user_preset(name, current_var.get()):\n                    messagebox.showinfo(\"Success\", f\"Saved '{name}' to My Presets\", parent=dialog)\n                else:\n                    messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Failed to save preset\", parent=dialog)\n        \n        ttk.Button(dialog, text=\"\u2b50 Save as Preset\", command=save_as_preset).pack(pady=10)\n        \n        # Buttons\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=10)\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            self._update_entry(resource_path, current_var.get())\n            dialog.destroy()\n        \n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=dialog.destroy).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)\n    \n    def _edit_with_presets(self, resource_path: str, current_value: str, preset_type: str):\n        \"\"\"Edit with preset dropdown for fonts, booleans, etc.\"\"\"\n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(f\"Edit {preset_type.title()} - {resource_path}\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        dialog.geometry(\"400x350\")\n        \n        # Current value\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Current Value:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=5)\n        current_var = tk.StringVar(value=current_value)\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=current_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        # Preset selection\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=f\"Choose {preset_type.title()} Preset:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=10)\n        \n        presets = get_all_presets()\n        if preset_type in presets:\n            preset_names = [name for name, _ in presets[preset_type]['items']]\n            preset_var = tk.StringVar()\n            \n            combo = ttk.Combobox(dialog, textvariable=preset_var, values=preset_names, width=35, state='readonly')\n            combo.pack(padx=10, pady=5)\n            \n            def on_preset_select(event):\n                selected = combo.get()\n                for name, val in presets[preset_type]['items']:\n                    if name == selected:\n                        current_var.set(val)\n                        break\n            \n            combo.bind('<<ComboboxSelected>>', on_preset_select)\n        \n        # Save as preset button\n        def save_as_preset():\n            name = simpledialog.askstring(\"Save Preset\", \"Enter preset name:\", parent=dialog)\n            if name:\n                if add_user_preset(name, current_var.get()):\n                    messagebox.showinfo(\"Success\", f\"Saved '{name}' to My Presets\", parent=dialog)\n                else:\n                    messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Failed to save preset\", parent=dialog)\n        \n        ttk.Button(dialog, text=\"\u2b50 Save as Preset\", command=save_as_preset).pack(pady=10)\n        \n        # Buttons\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=10)\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            self._update_entry(resource_path, current_var.get())\n            dialog.destroy()\n        \n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=dialog.destroy).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)\n    \n    def _edit_generic(self, resource_path: str, current_value: str):\n        \"\"\"Edit value with simple dialog.\"\"\"\n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(f\"Edit Resource - {resource_path}\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        dialog.geometry(\"400x250\")\n        \n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Value:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=5)\n        current_var = tk.StringVar(value=current_value)\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=current_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        # Save as preset button\n        def save_as_preset():\n            name = simpledialog.askstring(\"Save Preset\", \"Enter preset name:\", parent=dialog)\n            if name:\n                if add_user_preset(name, current_var.get()):\n                    messagebox.showinfo(\"Success\", f\"Saved '{name}' to My Presets\", parent=dialog)\n                else:\n                    messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Failed to save preset\", parent=dialog)\n        \n        ttk.Button(dialog, text=\"\u2b50 Save as Preset\", command=save_as_preset).pack(pady=10)\n        \n        # Buttons\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=10)\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            self._update_entry(resource_path, current_var.get())\n            dialog.destroy()\n        \n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=dialog.destroy).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)\n    \n    def _update_entry(self, resource_path: str, new_value: str):\n        \"\"\"Update an entry value.\"\"\"\n        # Update in parser\n        if self.parser.update_value(resource_path, new_value):\n            # Update in our list\n            for entry in self.entries:\n                if entry.resource_path == resource_path:\n                    entry.value = new_value\n                    break\n            \n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._on_filter_changed()  # Refresh display\n            self.set_status(f\"Updated {resource_path}\")\n    \n    def _manage_user_presets(self):\n        \"\"\"Show dialog to manage user presets.\"\"\"\n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"My Presets\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        dialog.geometry(\"500x400\")\n        \n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Your Custom Presets\", font=('Helvetica', 12, 'bold')).pack(pady=10)\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=f\"Saved in: {USER_PRESETS_FILE}\", foreground=\"gray\").pack()\n        \n        # Preset list\n        list_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        list_frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=10, pady=10)\n        \n        columns = ('name', 'value')\n        preset_tree = ttk.Treeview(list_frame, columns=columns, show='headings', height=12)\n        preset_tree.heading('name', text='Preset Name')\n        preset_tree.heading('value', text='Value')\n        preset_tree.column('name', width=150)\n        preset_tree.column('value', width=300)\n        \n        y_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(list_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=preset_tree.yview)\n        preset_tree.configure(yscrollcommand=y_scroll.set)\n        y_scroll.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)\n        preset_tree.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)\n        \n        # Load user presets\n        def refresh_presets():\n            for item in preset_tree.get_children():\n                preset_tree.delete(item)\n            \n            user_presets = get_user_presets_list()\n            for name, value in user_presets:\n                # Truncate long values for display\n                display_value = value[:50] + '...' if len(value) > 50 else value\n                preset_tree.insert('', 'end', values=(name, display_value))\n        \n        refresh_presets()\n        \n        # Buttons\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=10)\n        \n        def delete_selected():\n            selection = preset_tree.selection()\n            if selection:\n                item = selection[0]\n                values = preset_tree.item(item, 'values')\n                name = values[0]\n                if messagebox.askyesno(\"Confirm Delete\", f\"Delete preset '{name}'?\", parent=dialog):\n                    if delete_user_preset(name):\n                        refresh_presets()\n                        self.set_status(f\"Deleted preset '{name}'\")\n        \n        def add_new_preset():\n            name = simpledialog.askstring(\"New Preset\", \"Enter preset name:\", parent=dialog)\n            if name:\n                value = simpledialog.askstring(\"New Preset\", \"Enter preset value:\", parent=dialog)\n                if value:\n                    if add_user_preset(name, value):\n <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nKey-Value Editor Widget for KosXER\n\nSimple two-column editor for KEY=value files.\nGood for .env files, simple configs, shell exports, etc.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk, messagebox, filedialog\nfrom typing import Optional, List, Dict\n\nfrom gui.editor_base import EditorWidget\nfrom parsers.generic_kv_parser import GenericKVParser, KVEntry\n\n\nclass KVEditor(EditorWidget):\n    \"\"\"\n    Editor widget for key-value configuration files.\n    \n    Features:\n    - Two-column editable treeview (Key, Value)\n    - Add/Delete rows\n    - Import/Export functionality\n    - Search/filter\n    - Intelligent quote handling\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, parent, main_window=None, filepath: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs):\n        self.parser = GenericKVParser()\n        self.entries: List[KVEntry] = []\n        self.filtered_entries: List[KVEntry] = []\n        self._edit_popup: Optional[tk.Toplevel] = None\n        \n        super().__init__(parent, main_window, filepath, **kwargs)\n    \n    def _create_editor_widgets(self):\n        \"\"\"Create the KV editor UI.\"\"\"\n        # Filter frame\n        filter_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        filter_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        ttk.Label(filter_frame, text=\"Search:\").pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        self.filter_var = tk.StringVar()\n        self.filter_var.trace('w', self._on_filter_changed)\n        ttk.Entry(filter_frame, textvariable=self.filter_var, width=30).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        ttk.Button(filter_frame, text=\"Clear\", command=self._clear_filter).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Treeview frame\n        tree_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        tree_frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, pady=5)\n        \n        # Treeview\n        columns = ('key', 'value', 'export')\n        self.tree = ttk.Treeview(tree_frame, columns=columns, show='headings')\n        \n        self.tree.heading('key', text='Key')\n        self.tree.heading('value', text='Value')\n        self.tree.heading('export', text='Export')\n        \n        self.tree.column('key', width=200)\n        self.tree.column('value', width=400)\n        self.tree.column('export', width=60)\n        \n        # Import/Export\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Import\", command=self._import_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Export\", command=self._export_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Bindings\n        self.tree.bind('<Double-1>', self._on_double_click)\n        self.tree.bind('<Delete>', lambda e: self._delete_selected())\n        self.tree.bind('<Return>', lambda e: self._edit_selected())\n    \n    def _populate_tree(self):\n        \"\"\"Populate treeview with entries.\"\"\"\n        # Clear existing\n        for item in self.tree.get_children():\n            self.tree.delete(item)\n        \n        # Add filtered entries\n        for entry in self.filtered_entries:\n            export_mark = '\u2713' if entry.is_export else ''\n            self.tree.insert('', 'end', values=(\n                entry.key,\n                entry.value,\n                export_mark\n            ))\n    \n    def _on_filter_changed(self, *args):\n        \"\"\"Apply filter.\"\"\"\n        filter_text = self.filter_var.get().lower()\n        \n        if not filter_text:\n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        else:\n            self.filtered_entries = [\n                e for e in self.entries \n                if filter_text in e.key.lower() or filter_text in e.value.lower()\n            ]\n        \n        self._populate_tree()\n        self.set_status(f\"Showing {len(self.filtered_entries)} of {len(self.entries)} entries\")\n    \n    def _clear_filter(self):\n        \"\"\"Clear filter.\"\"\"\n        self.filter_var.set('')\n        self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        self._populate_tree()\n    \n    def _on_double_click(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Handle double click for editing.\"\"\"\n        self._edit_selected()\n    \n    def _add_row(self):\n        \"\"\"Add new key-value row.\"\"\"\n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"Add Entry\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        \n        # Key field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Key:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        key_var = tk.StringVar()\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=key_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Value field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Value:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        value_var = tk.StringVar()\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=value_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Export checkbox\n        export_var = tk.BooleanVar(value=False)\n        ttk.Checkbutton(dialog, text=\"Export (bash)\", variable=export_var).pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            key = key_var.get().strip()\n            value = value_var.get().strip()\n            \n            if not key:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Key is required\")\n                return\n            \n            # Check for duplicate\n            if any(e.key == key for e in self.entries):\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Key '{key}' already exists\")\n                return\n            \n            entry = KVEntry(key=key, value=value, is_export=export_var.get())\n            self.entries.append(entry)\n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._populate_tree()\n            self.set_status(f\"Added: {key}\")\n            dialog.destroy()\n        \n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(pady=10)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=dialog.destroy).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n    \n    def _delete_selected(self):\n        \"\"\"Delete selected row(s).\"\"\"\n        selection = self.tree.selection()\n        if not selection:\n            messagebox.showwarning(\"No Selection\", \"Please select a row to delete\")\n            return\n        \n        if messagebox.askyesno(\"Confirm\", \"Delete selected row(s)?\"):\n            for item_id in selection:\n                values = self.tree.item(item_id, 'values')\n                key = values[0]\n                \n                # Remove from entries\n                self.entries = [e for e in self.entries if e.key != key]\n            \n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._populate_tree()\n            self.set_status(f\"Deleted {len(selection)} row(s)\")\n    \n    def _edit_selected(self):\n        \"\"\"Edit selected row.\"\"\"\n        selection = self.tree.selection()\n        if not selection:\n            return\n        \n        item_id = selection[0]\n        values = self.tree.item(item_id, 'values')\n        old_key = values[0]\n        old_value = values[1]\n        old_export = values[2] == '\u2713'\n        \n        # Find entry\n        entry = next((e for e in self.entries if e.key == old_key), None)\n        if not entry:\n            return\n        \n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"Edit Entry\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        \n        # Key field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Key:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        key_var = tk.StringVar(value=old_key)\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=key_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Value field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Value:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        value_var = tk.StringVar(value=old_value)\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=value_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Export checkbox\n        export_var = tk.BooleanVar(value=old_export)\n        ttk.Checkbutton(dialog, text=\"Export (bash)\", variable=export_var).pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            new_key = key_var.get().strip()\n            new_value = value_var.get().strip()\n            \n            if not new_key:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Key is required\")\n                return\n            \n            # Check if key changed and new key exists\n            if new_key != old_key and any(e.key == new_key for e in self.entries):\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Key '{new_key}' already exists\")\n                return\n            \n            # Update entry\n            entry.key = new_key\n            entry.value = new_value\n            entry.is_export = export_var.get()\n            \n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._on_filter_changed()\n            self.set_status(f\"Updated: {new_key}\")\n            dialog.destroy()\n        \n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(pady=10)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=dialog.destroy).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n    \n    def _import_file(self):\n        \"\"\"Import from another file.\"\"\"\n        filepath = filedialog.askopenfilename(\n            title=\"Import Key-Value File\",\n            filetypes=[(\"All Files\", \"*.*\"), (\"Env Files\", \"*.env\"), (\"Config\", \"*.conf\")]\n        )\n        if not filepath:\n            return\n        \n        try:\n            new_parser = GenericKVParser()\n            new_entries = new_parser.parse_file(filepath)\n            \n            # Merge or replace\n            if messagebox.askyesno(\"Import\", \"Replace current entries?\"):\n                self.entries = new_entries\n            else:\n                # Merge, skipping duplicates\n                existing_keys = {e.key for e in self.entries}\n                for entry in new_entries:\n                    if entry.key not in existing_keys:\n                        self.entries.append(entry)\n            \n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._populate_tree()\n            self.set_status(f\"Imported {len(new_entries)} entries from {filepath}\")\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Import Error\", str(e))\n    \n    def _export_file(self):\n        \"\"\"Export to another file.\"\"\"\n        filepath = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(\n            title=\"Export Key-Value File\",\n            defaultextension=\".env\",\n            filetypes=[(\"Env File\", \"*.env\"), (\"Config\", \"*.conf\"), (\"All\", \"*.*\")]\n        )\n        if not filepath:\n            return\n        \n        try:\n            # Update parser entries\n            self.parser.entries = self.entries\n            self.parser.write_back(filepath)\n            self.set_status(f\"Exported to {filepath}\")\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Export Error\", str(e))\n    \n    # files.\n\nSupported Formats:\n  \u2022 .Xresources / .Xdefaults  - X11 resources\n  \u2022 menu.xml / rc.xml          - OpenBox\n  \u2022 KosDWM config & menus     - Dynamic window manager\n  \u2022 .conf / .env / .rc        - Key-value configs\n  \u2022 .bashrc / .zshrc          - Shell configs\n\nKeyboard Shortcuts:\n  Ctrl+O  Open file\n  Ctrl+S  Save\n  Ctrl+Q  Quit\n  Ctrl+B  Toggle file browser\n  Ctrl+H  Toggle hidden files\n  F5      Refresh\n\"\"\")\n        text.config(state=tk.DISABLED)\n    \n    def _create_statusbar(self):\n        \"\"\"Create status bar.\"\"\"\n        self.statusbar = ttk.Frame(self.root, relief=tk.SUNKEN, borderwidth=1)\n        self.statusbar.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)\n        \n        self.status_file = ttk.Label(self.statusbar, text=\"No file open\", anchor=tk.W, width=40)\n        self.status_file.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        ttk.Separator(self.statusbar, orient=tk.VERTICAL).pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.Y, padx=5)\n        \n        self.status_parser = ttk.Label(self.statusbar, text=\"\", width=25)\n        self.status_parser.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        self.status_modified = anchor=tk.E, width=20)\n        self.status_pos.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)\n    \n    def _bind_shortcuts(self):\n        \"\"\"Bind keyboard shortcuts.\"\"\"\n        self.root.bind(\"<Control-n>\", lambda e: self._file_new())\n        self.root.bind(\"<Control-o>\", lambda e: self._file_open())\n        self.root.bind(\"<Control-s>\", lambda e: self._file_save())\n        self.root.bind(\"<Control-S>\", lambda e: self._file_save_as())\n        self.root.bind(\"<Control-w>\", lambda e: self._close_current_tab())\n        self.root.bind(\"<Control-b>\", lambda e: self._toggle_file_browser())\n        self.root.bind(\"<Control-h>\", lambda e: self._toggle_hidden_files())\n        self.root.bind(\"<F5>\", lambda e: self._refresh_browser())\n        self.root.bind(\"<Control-q>\", lambda e: self._on_close())\n    \n    def _toggle_hidden_files(self):\n        \"\"\"Toggle hidden files display.\"\"\"\n        current = self.show_hidden_var.get()\n        self.show_hidden_var.set(not current)\n        if hasattr(self, 'file_browser'):\n            self.file_browser.set_show_hidden(self.show_hidden_var.get())\n    \n    def _refresh_browser(self):\n        \"\"\"Refresh file browser.\"\"\"\n        if hasattr(self, 'file_browser'):\n            self.file_browser.refresh()\n    \n    def _open_file(self, filepath: str):\n        \"\"\"Open a file.\"\"\"\n        filepath = str(filepath)\n        \n        # Check if already open\n        if filepath in self.open_files:\n            for i, tab in enumerate(self.notebook.tabs()):\n                if self.notebook.tab(tab, \"text\") == Path(filepath).name:\n                    self.notebook.select(i)\n                    return\n        \n
