type: {filepath}\")\n                return\n            \n            # Create appropriate editor\n            if parser_class == XResourcesParser:\n                editor = XResourcesEditor(self.notebook, self, filepath)\n            elif parser_class == OpenBoxMenuParser:\n                editor = OpenBoxEditor(self.notebook, self, filepath)\n            elif parser_class == GenericKVParser:\n                editor = KVEditor(self.notebook, self, filepath)\n            elif parser_class == KosDWMConfigParser:\n                editor = KosDWMConfigEditor(self.notebook, self, filepath)\n            elif parser_class == KosDWMMenuParser:\n                editor = KosDWMMenuEditor(self.notebook, self, filepath)\n            else:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"No editor for: {filepath}\")\n                return\n            \n            # Load file\n            with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                content = f.read()\n            editor.load_data(content)\n            \n            # Add tab\n            tab_text = Path(filepath).name\n            if len(tab_text) > 20:\n                tab_text = tab_text[:17] + \"...\"\n            \n            self.notebook.add(editor, text=tab_text)\n            self.notebook.select(editor)\n            \n filepath: str, parser_desc: str):\n        \"\"\"Update status bar.\"\"\"\n        self.status_file.config(text=f\"\ud83d\udcc4 {Path(filepath).name}\")\n (\"KosDWM\", \"config.json\"),\n            (\"All\", \"*.*\")\n        ]\n        \n        filepath = filedialog.askopenfilename(title=\"Open File\", filetypes=filetypes)\n        if filepath:\n            self._open_file(filepath)\n    \n    def _file_save(self):\n        \"\"\"Save current file.\"\"\"\n        if not self.current_file:\n            self._file_save_as()\n            return\n open(self.current_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                f.write(content)\n            \n            editor.mark_dirty(False)\n            self.status_modified.config(text=\"\u2713 Saved\")\n            self.root.after(2000, lambda: self.status_modified.config(text=\"\"))\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Save Error\", str(e))\n    \n    def _file_save_as(self):\n        \"\"\"Save as dialog.\"\"\"\n        if not self.current_file:\n            return\n        \n        filepath = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(\n self.notebook.forget(current)\n    \n    def _edit_undo(self):\n        \"\"\"Undo.\"\"\"\n        editor = self.open_files.get(self.current_file)\n        if editor and hasattr(editor, 'undo'):\n            editor.undo()\n    \n    def _edit_redo(self):\n        \"\"\"Redo.\"\"\"\n        editor = self.open_files.get(self.current_file)\n        if editor and hasattr(editor, 'redo'):\n            editor.redo()\n    \n    def _edit_cut(self):\n        \"\"\"Cut.\"\"\"\n        self.root.focus_get().event_generate(\"<<Cut>>\")\n    \n    def _edit_copy(self):\n        \"\"\"Copy.\"\"\"\n        self.root.focus_get().event_generate(\"<<Copy>>\")\n    \n    def _edit_paste(self):\n        \"\"\"Paste.\"\"\"\n        self.root.focus_get().event_generate(\"<<Paste>>\")\n    \n    def > """
> Key-Value Editor Widget for KosXER
> 
> Simple two-column editor for KEY=value files.
> Good for .env files, simple configs, shell exports, etc.
> """

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nKey-Value Editor Widget for KosXER\n\nSimple two-column editor for KEY=value files.\nGood for .env files, simple configs, shell exports, etc.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk, messagebox, filedialog\nfrom typing import Optional, List, Dict\n\nfrom gui.editor_base import EditorWidget\nfrom parsers.generic_kv_parser import GenericKVParser, KVEntry\n\n\nclass KVEditor(EditorWidget):\n    \"\"\"\n    Editor widget for key-value configuration files.\n    \n    Features:\n    - Two-column editable treeview (Key, Value)\n    - Add/Delete rows\n    - Import/Export functionality\n    - Search/filter\n    - Intelligent quote handling\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, parent, main_window=None, filepath: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs):\n        self.parser = GenericKVParser()\n        self.entries: List[KVEntry] = []\n        self.filtered_entries: List[KVEntry] = []\n        self._edit_popup: Optional[tk.Toplevel] = None\n        \n        super().__init__(parent, main_window, filepath, **kwargs)\n    \n    def _create_editor_widgets(self):\n        \"\"\"Create the KV editor UI.\"\"\"\n        # Filter frame\n        filter_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        filter_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        ttk.Label(filter_frame, text=\"Search:\").pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        self.filter_var = tk.StringVar()\n        self.filter_var.trace('w', self._on_filter_changed)\n        ttk.Entry(filter_frame, textvariable=self.filter_var, width=30).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        ttk.Button(filter_frame, text=\"Clear\", command=self._clear_filter).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Treeview frame\n        tree_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        tree_frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, pady=5)\n        \n        # Treeview\n        columns = ('key', 'value', 'export')\n        self.tree = ttk.Treeview(tree_frame, columns=columns, show='headings')\n        \n        self.tree.heading('key', text='Key')\n        self.tree.heading('value', text='Value')\n        self.tree.heading('export', text='Export')\n        \n        self.tree.column('key', width=200)\n        self.tree.column('value', width=400)\n        self.tree.column('export', width=60)\n        \n        # Scrollbars\n        y_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.tree.yview)\n        x_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.tree.xview)\n        self.tree.configure(yscrollcommand=y_scroll.set, xscrollcommand=x_scroll.set)\n        \n        y_scroll.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)\n        x_scroll.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)\n        self.tree.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)\n        \n        # Button frame\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        # Row operations\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Add Row\", command=self._add_row).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Delete Selected\", command=self._delete_selected).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Edit Selected\", command=self._edit_selected).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        ttk.Separator(btn_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL).pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.Y, padx=10)\n        \n        # Import/Export\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Import\", command=self._import_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Export\", command=self._export_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Bindings\n        self.tree.bind('<Double-1>', self._on_double_click)\n        self.tree.bind('<Delete>', lambda e: self._delete_selected())\n        self.tree.bind('<Return>', lambda e: self._edit_selected())\n    \n    def _populate_tree(self):\n        \"\"\"Populate treeview with entries.\"\"\"\n        # Clear existing\n        for item in self.tree.get_children():\n            self.tree.delete(item)\n        \n        # Add filtered entries\n        for entry in self.filtered_entries:\n            export_mark = '\u2713' if entry.is_export else ''\n            self.tree.insert('', 'end', values=(\n                entry.key,\n                entry.value,\n                export_mark\n            ))\n    \n    def _on_filter_changed(self, *args):\n        \"\"\"Apply filter.\"\"\"\n        filter_text = self.filter_var.get().lower()\n        \n        if not filter_text:\n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        else:\n            self.filtered_entries = [\n                e for e in self.entries \n                if filter_text in e.key.lower() or filter_text in e.value.lower()\n            ]\n        \n        self._populate_tree()\n        self.set_status(f\"Showing {len(self.filtered_entries)} of {len(self.entries)} entries\")\n    \n    def _clear_filter(self):\n        \"\"\"Clear filter.\"\"\"\n        self.filter_var.set('')\n        self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        self._populate_tree()\n    \n    def _on_double_click(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Handle double click for editing.\"\"\"\n        self._edit_selected()\n    \n    def _add_row(self):\n        \"\"\"Add new key-value row.\"\"\"\n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"Add Entry\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        \n        # Key field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Key:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        key_var = tk.StringVar()\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=key_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Value field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Value:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        value_var = tk.StringVar()\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=value_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Export checkbox\n        export_var = tk.BooleanVar(value=False)\n        ttk.Checkbutton(dialog, text=\"Export (bash)\", variable=export_var).pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            key = key_var.get().strip()\n            value = value_var.get().strip()\n            \n            if not key:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Key is required\")\n                return\n            \n            # Check for duplicate\n            if any(e.key == key for e in self.entries):\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Key '{key}' already exists\")\n                return\n            \n            entry = KVEntry(key=key, value=value, is_export=export_var.get())\n            self.entries.append(entry)\n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._populate_tree()\n            self.set_status(f\"Added: {key}\")\n            dialog.destroy()\n        \n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(pady=10)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=dialog.destroy).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n    \n    def _delete_selected(self):\n        \"\"\"Delete selected row(s).\"\"\"\n        selection = self.tree.selection()\n        if not selection:\n            messagebox.showwarning(\"No Selection\", \"Please select a row to delete\")\n            return\n        \n        if messagebox.askyesno(\"Confirm\", \"Delete selected row(s)?\"):\n            for item_id in selection:\n                values = self.tree.item(item_id, 'values')\n                key = values[0]\n                \n                # Remove from entries\n                self.entries = [e for e in self.entries if e.key != key]\n            \n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._populate_tree()\n            self.set_status(f\"Deleted {len(selection)} row(s)\")\n    \n    def _edit_selected(self):\n        \"\"\"Edit selected row.\"\"\"\n        selection = self.tree.selection()\n        if not selection:\n            return\n        \n        item_id = selection[0]\n        values = self.tree.item(item_id, 'values')\n        old_key = values[0]\n        old_value = values[1]\n        old_export = values[2] == '\u2713'\n        \n        # Find entry\n        entry = next((e for e in self.entries if e.key == old_key), None)\n        if not entry:\n            return\n        \n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"Edit Entry\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        \n        # Key field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Key:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        key_var = tk.StringVar(value=old_key)\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=key_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Value field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Value:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        value_var = tk.StringVar(value=old_value)\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=value_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Export checkbox\n        export_var = tk.BooleanVar(value=old_export)\n        ttk.Checkbutton(dialog, text=\"Export (bash)\", variable=export_var).pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            new_key = key_var.get().strip()\n            new_value = value_var.get().strip()\n            \n            if not new_key:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Key is required\")\n                return\n            \n            # Check if key changed and new key exists\n            if new_key != old_key and any(e.key == new_key for e in self.entries):\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Key '{new_key}' already exists\")\n                return\n            \n            # Update entry\n            entry.key = new_key\n            entry.value = new_value\n            entry.is_export = export_var.get()\n            \n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._on_filter_changed()\n            self.set_status(f\"Updated: {new_key}\")\n            dialog.destroy()\n        \n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(pady=10)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=dialog.destroy).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n    \n    def _import_file(self):\n        \"\"\"Import from another file.\"\"\"\n        filepath = filedialog.askopenfilename(\n            title=\"Import Key-Value File\",\n            filetypes=[(\"All Files\", \"*.*\"), (\"Env Files\", \"*.env\"), (\"Config\", \"*.conf\")]\n        )\n        if not filepath:\n            return\n        \n        try:\n            new_parser = GenericKVParser()\n            new_entries = new_parser.parse_file(filepath)\n            \n            # Merge or replace\n            if messagebox.askyesno(\"Import\", \"Replace current entries?\"):\n                self.entries = new_entries\n            else:\n                # Merge, skipping duplicates\n                existing_keys = {e.key for e in self.entries}\n                for entry in new_entries:\n                    if entry.key not in existing_keys:\n                        self.entries.append(entry)\n            \n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._populate_tree()\n            self.set_status(f\"Imported {len(new_entries)} entries from {filepath}\")\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Import Error\", str(e))\n    \n    def _export_file(self):\n        \"\"\"Export to another file.\"\"\"\n        filepath = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(\n            title=\"Export Key-Value File\",\n            defaultextension=\".env\",\n            filetypes=[(\"Env File\", \"*.env\"), (\"Config\", \"*.conf\"), (\"All\", \"*.*\")]\n        )\n        if not filepath:\n            return\n        \n        try:\n            # Update parser entries\n            self.parser.entries = self.entries\n            self.parser.write_back(filepath)\n            self.set_status(f\"Exported to {filepath}\")\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Export Error\", str(e))\n    \n    # Required abstract methods\n    \n    def load_data(self, data: str):\n        \"\"\"Load key-value content.\"\"\"\n        self.entries = self.parser.parse(data)\n        self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        self._original_data = data\n        self._populate_tree()\n        self.mark_dirty(False)\n        self.set_status(f\"Loaded {len(self.entries)} entries\")\n    \n    def get_data(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get key-value content.\"\"\"\n        self.parser.entries = self.entries\n        return self.parser.write_back()\n    \n    def validate(self) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n        \"\"\"Validate key-value data.\"\"\"\n        if not self.entries:\n            return True, \"\"  # Empty is valid\n        \n        # Check for duplicate keys\n        keys = [e.key for e in self.entries]\n        if len(keys) != len(set(keys)):\n            return False, \"Duplicate keys found\"\n        \n        # Check for invalid key names\n        for entry in self.entries:\n            if not entry.key:\n                return False, \"Empty key found\"\n            if ' ' in entry.key:\n                return False, f\"Key contains space: {entry.key}\"\n        \n        return True, \"\"\n", "sessionId": 327, "rowId": 1, "timestamp": 1784290160.4889133, "date": "2026-07-17", "name": "ReadFile"} -->

Check if key changed and new key exists\n            if new_key != old_key and any(e.key == new_key for e in self.entries):\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Key '{new_key}' already exists\")\n                return\n            \n            # #!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> Key-Value Editor Widget for KosXER
> 
> Simple two-column editor for KEY=value files.
> Good for .env files, simple configs, shell exports, etc.
> """
> 
> import tkinter as tk
> from tkinter import ttk, messagebox, filedialog
> from typing import Optional, List, Dict
> 
> from gui.editor_base import EditorWidget
> from parsers.generic_kv_parser import GenericKVParser, KVEntry
> 
> 
> class KVEditor(EditorWidget):
>     """
>     Editor widget for key-value configuration files.
>     
>     Features:

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nKey-Value Editor Widget for KosXER\n\nSimple two-column editor for KEY=value files.\nGood for .env files, simple configs, shell exports, etc.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk, messagebox, filedialog\nfrom typing import Optional, List, Dict\n\nfrom gui.editor_base import EditorWidget\nfrom parsers.generic_kv_parser import GenericKVParser, KVEntry\n\n\nclass KVEditor(EditorWidget):\n    \"\"\"\n    Editor widget for key-value configuration files.\n    \n    Features:\n        self._edit_popup: Optional[tk.Toplevel] = None\n        self._dialog_open = False  # Prevent duplicate dialogs\n        self._delete_in_progress = False  # Prevent duplicate deletes\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, parent, main_window=None, filepath: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs):\n        self.parser = GenericKVParser()\n        self.entries: List[KVEntry] = []\n        self.filtered_entries: List[KVEntry] = []\n        self._edit_popup: Optional[tk.Toplevel] = None\n        self._dialog_open = False  # Prevent duplicate dialogs\n        \n        super().__init__(parent, main_window, filepath, **kwargs)\n    \n    def _create_editor_widgets(self):\n        \"\"\"Create the KV editor UI.\"\"\"\n        # Filter frame\n        filter_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        filter_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        ttk.Label(filter_frame, text=\"Search:\").pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        self.filter_var = tk.StringVar()\n        self.filter_var.trace('w', self._on_filter_changed)\n        ttk.Entry(filter_frame, textvariable=self.filter_var, width=30).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        ttk.Button(filter_frame, text=\"Clear\", command=self._clear_filter).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Treeview frame\n        tree_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        tree_frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, pady=5)\n        \n        # Treeview\n        columns = ('key', 'value', 'export')\n        self.tree = ttk.Treeview(tree_frame, columns=columns, show='headings')\n        \n        self.tree.heading('key', text='Key')\n        self.tree.heading('value', text='Value')\n        self.tree.heading('export', text='Export')\n        \n        self.tree.column('key', width=200)\n        self.tree.column('value', width=400)\n        self.tree.column('export', width=60)\n        \n        # Scrollbars\n        y_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.tree.yview)\n        x_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.tree.xview)\n        self.tree.configure(yscrollcommand=y_scroll.set, xscrollcommand=x_scroll.set)\n        \n        y_scroll.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)\n        x_scroll.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)\n        self.tree.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)\n        \n        # Button frame\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        # Row operations\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Add Row\", command=self._add_row).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Delete Selected\", command=self._delete_selected).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Edit Selected\", command=self._edit_selected).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        ttk.Separator(btn_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL).pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.Y, padx=10)\n        \n        # Import/Export\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Import\", command=self._import_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Export\", command=self._export_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Bindings\n        self.tree.bind('<Double-1>', self._on_double_click)\n        self.tree.bind('<Delete>', lambda e: self._delete_selected())\n        self.tree.bind('<Return>', lambda e: self._edit_selected())\n    \n    def _populate_tree(self):\n        \"\"\"Populate treeview with entries.\"\"\"\n        # Clear existing\n        for item in self.tree.get_children():\n            self.tree.delete(item)\n        \n        # Add filtered entries\n        for entry in self.filtered_entries:\n            export_mark = '\u2713' if entry.is_export else ''\n            self.tree.insert('', 'end', values=(\n                entry.key,\n                entry.value,\n                export_mark\n            ))\n    \n    def _on_filter_changed(self, *args):\n        \"\"\"Apply filter.\"\"\"\n        filter_text = self.filter_var.get().lower()\n        \n        if not filter_text:\n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        else:\n            self.filtered_entries = [\n                e for e in self.entries \n                if filter_text in e.key.lower() or filter_text in e.value.lower()\n            ]\n        \n        self._populate_tree()\n        self.set_status(f\"Showing {len(self.filtered_entries)} of {len(self.entries)} entries\")\n    \n    def _clear_filter(self):\n        \"\"\"Clear filter.\"\"\"\n        self.filter_var.set('')\n        self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        self._populate_tree()\n    \n    def _on_double_click(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Handle double click for editing.\"\"\"\n        self._edit_selected()\n    \n    def _add_row(self):\n        \"\"\"Add new key-value row.\"\"\"\n        # Prevent duplicate dialogs\n        if self._dialog_open:\n            return\n        self._dialog_open = True\n        \n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"Add Entry\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        dialog.protocol(\"WM_DELETE_WINDOW\", lambda: self._close_dialog(dialog))\n        \n        # Key field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Key:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        key_var = tk.StringVar()\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=key_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Value field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Value:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        value_var = tk.StringVar()\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=value_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Export checkbox\n        export_var = tk.BooleanVar(value=False)\n        ttk.Checkbutton(dialog, text=\"Export (bash)\", variable=export_var).pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        # Track if already processed to prevent double-add\n        self._add_processed = False\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            # Prevent double execution\n            if self._add_processed:\n                return\n            self._add_processed = True\n            \n            key = key_var.get().strip()\n            value = value_var.get().strip()\n            \n            if not key:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Key is required\")\n                self._add_processed = False\n                return\n            \n            # Check for duplicate\n            if any(e.key == key for e in self.entries):\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Key '{key}' already exists\")\n                self._add_processed = False\n                return\n            \n            entry = KVEntry(key=key, value=value, is_export=export_var.get())\n            self.entries.append(entry)\n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._populate_tree()\n            self.set_status(f\"Added: {key}\")\n            self._close_dialog(dialog)\n        \n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(pady=10)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=lambda: self._close_dialog(dialog)).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Center dialog\n        dialog.update_idletasks()\n        x = self.winfo_rootx() + (self.winfo_width() - dialog.winfo_width()) // 2\n        y = self.winfo_rooty() + (self.winfo_height() - dialog.winfo_height()) // 2\n        dialog.geometry(f\"+{x}+{y}\")\n    \n    def _close_dialog(self, dialog):\n        \"\"\"Close dialog and reset flag.\"\"\"\n        self._dialog_open = False\n        dialog.destroy()\n    \n    def _delete_selected(self):\n        \"\"\"Delete selected row(s).\"\"\"\n        selection = self.tree.selection()\n        if not selection:\n            messagebox.showwarning(\"No Selection\", \"Please select a row to delete\")\n            return\n        \n        if messagebox.askyesno(\"Confirm\", \"Delete selected row(s)?\"):\n            for item_id in selection:\n                values = self.tree.item(item_id, 'values')\n                key = values[0]\n                \n                # Remove from entries\n                self.entries = [e for e in self.entries if e.key != key]\n            \n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._populate_tree()\n            self.set_status(f\"Deleted {len(selection)} row(s)\")\n    \n    def _edit_selected(self):\n        \"\"\"Edit selected row.\"\"\"\n        if self._dialog_open:\n            return\n        self._dialog_open = True\n        \n        selection = self.tree.selection()\n        if not selection:\n            self._dialog_open = False\n            return\n        \n        item_id = selection[0]\n        values = self.tree.item(item_id, 'values')\n        old_key = values[0]\n        old_value = values[1]\n        old_export = values[2] == '\u2713'\n        \n        # Find entry\n        entry = next((e for e in self.entries if e.key == old_key), None)\n        if not entry:\n            self._dialog_open = False\n            return\n        \n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"Edit Entry\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        dialog.protocol(\"WM_DELETE_WINDOW\", lambda: self._close_dialog(dialog))\n        \n        # Key field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Key:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        key_var = tk.StringVar(value=old_key)\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=key_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Value field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Value:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        value_var = tk.StringVar(value=old_value)\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=value_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Export checkbox\n        export_var = tk.BooleanVar(value=old_export)\n        ttk.Checkbutton(dialog, text=\"Export (bash)\", variable=export_var).pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            new_key = key_var.get().strip()\n            new_value = value_var.get().strip()\n            \n            if not new_key:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Key is required\")\n                return\n            \n            # Check if key changed and new key exists\n            if new_key != old_key and any(e.key == new_key for e in self.entries):\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Key '{new_key}' already exists\")\n                return\n            \n            # Update entry\n            entry.key = new_key\n            entry.value = new_value\n            entry.is_export = export_var.get()\n            \n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._on_filter_changed()\n            self.set_status(f\"Updated: {new_key}\")\n            self._close_dialog(dialog)\n        \n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(pady=10)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=lambda: self._close_dialog(dialog)).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Center dialog\n        dialog.update_idletasks()\n        x = self.winfo_rootx() + (self.winfo_width() - dialog.winfo_width()) // 2\n        y = self.winfo_rooty() + (self.winfo_height() - dialog.winfo_height()) // 2\n        dialog.geometry(f\"+{x}+{y}\")\n    \n    def _import_file(self):\n        \"\"\"Import from another file.\"\"\"\n        filepath = filedialog.askopenfilename(\n            title=\"Import Key-Value File\",\n            filetypes=[(\"All Files\", \"*.*\"), (\"Env Files\", \"*.env\"), (\"Config\", \"*.conf\")]\n        )\n        if not filepath:\n            return\n        \n        try:\n            new_parser = GenericKVParser()\n            new_entries = new_parser.parse_file(filepath)\n            \n            # Merge or replace\n            if messagebox.askyesno(\"Import\", \"Replace current entries?\"):\n                self.entries = new_entries\n            else:\n                # Merge, skipping duplicates\n                existing_keys = {e.key for e in self.entries}\n                for entry in new_entries:\n                    if entry.key not in existing_keys:\n                        self.entries.append(entry)\n            \n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._populate_tree()\n            self.set_status(f\"Imported {len(new_entries)} entries from {filepath}\")\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Import Error\", str(e))\n    \n    def _export_file(self):\n        \"\"\"Export to another file.\"\"\"\n        filepath = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(\n            title=\"Export Key-Value File\",\n            defaultextension=\".env\",\n            filetypes=[(\"Env File\", \"*.env\"), (\"Config\", \"*.conf\"), (\"All\", \"*.*\")]\n        )\n        if not filepath:\n            return\n        \n        try:\n            # Update parser entries\n            self.parser.entries = self.entries\n            self.parser.write_back(filepath)\n            self.set_status(f\"Exported to {filepath}\")\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Export Error\", str(e))\n    \n    # Required abstract methods\n    \n    def load_data(self, data: str):\n        \"\"\"Load key-value content.\"\"\"\n        self.entries = self.parser.parse(data)\n        self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        self._original_data = data\n        self._populate_tree()\n        self.mark_dirty(False)\n        self.set_status(f\"Loaded {len(self.entries)} entries\")\n    \n    def get_data(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get key-value content.\"\"\"\n        self.parser.entries = self.entries\n        return self.parser.write_back()\n    \n    def validate(self) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n        \"\"\"Validate key-value data.\"\"\"\n        if not self.entries:\n            return True, \"\"  # Empty is valid\n        \n        # Check for duplicate keys\n        keys = [e.key for e in self.entries]\n        if len(keys) != len(set(keys)):\n            return False, \"Duplicate keys found\"\n        \n        # Check for invalid key names\n        for entry in self.entries:\n            if not entry.key:\n                return False, \"Empty key found\"\n            if ' ' in entry.key:\n                return False, f\"Key contains space: {entry.key}\"\n        \n        return True, \"\"\n", "sessionId": 327, "rowId": 1, "timestamp": 1784290214.8131142, "date": "2026-07-17", "name": "ReadFile"} -->

Scrollbars\n        y_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.tree.yview)\n        x_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.tree.xview)\n        self.tree.configure(yscrollcommand=y_scroll.set, xscrollcommand=x_scroll.set)\n        \n        y_scroll.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)\n        x_scroll.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)\n        self.tree.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)\n        \n        # Button frame\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        # Row operations\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Add Row\", command=self._add_row).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Delete Selected\", command=self._delete_selected).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Edit Selected\", command=self._edit_selected).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        ttk.Separator(btn_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL).pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.Y, padx=10)\n        \n        # Import/Export\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Import\", command=self._import_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Export\", command=self._export_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Bindings\n        self.tree.bind('<Double-1>', self._on_double_click)\n        self.tree.bind('<Delete>', lambda e: self._delete_selected())\n        self.tree.bind('<Return>', lambda e: self._edit_selected())\n    \n    def _populate_tree(self):\n        \"\"\"Populate treeview with entries.\"\"\"\n        # Clear existing\n        for item in self.tree.get_children():\n            self.tree.delete(item)\n        \n        # Add filtered entries\n        for entry in self.filtered_entries:\n            export_mark = '\u2713' if entry.is_export else ''\n            self.tree.insert('', 'end', values=(\n                entry.key,\n                entry.value,\n                export_mark\n            ))\n    \n    def _on_filter_changed(self, *args):\n        \"\"\"Apply filter.\"\"\"\n        filter_text = self.filter_var.get().lower()\n        \n        if not filter_text:\n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        else:\n            self.filtered_entries = [\n                e for e in self.entries \n                if filter_text in e.key.lower() or filter_text in e.value.lower()\n            ]\n        \n        self._populate_tree()\n        self.set_status(f\"Showing {len(self.filtered_entries)} of {len(self.entries)} entries\")\n    \n    def _clear_filter(self):\n        \"\"\"Clear filter.\"\"\"\n        self.filter_var.set('')\n        self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        self._populate_tree()\n    \n    def _on_double_click(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Handle double click for editing.\"\"\"\n        self._edit_selected()\n    \n    def _add_row(self):\n        \"\"\"Add new key-value row.\"\"\"\n        # Prevent duplicate dialogs\n        if self._dialog_open:\n            return\n        self._dialog_open = True\n        \n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"Add Entry\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        dialog.protocol(\"WM_DELETE_WINDOW\", lambda: self._close_dialog(dialog))\n        \n        # Key field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Key:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        key_var = tk.StringVar()\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=key_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Value field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Value:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        value_var = tk.StringVar()\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=value_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Export checkbox\n        export_var = tk.BooleanVar(value=False)\n        ttk.Checkbutton(dialog, text=\"Export (bash)\", variable=export_var).pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        # Track if already processed to prevent double-add\n        self._add_processed = False\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            # Prevent double execution\n            if self._add_processed:\n                return\n            self._add_processed = True\n            \n            key = key_var.get().strip()\n            value = value_var.get().strip()\n            \n            if not key:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Key is required\")\n                self._add_processed = False\n                return\n            \n            # Check for duplicate\n            if any(e.key == key for e in self.entries):\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Key '{key}' already exists\")\n                self._add_processed = False\n                return\n            \n            entry = KVEntry(key=key, value=value, is_export=export_var.get())\n            self.entries.append(entry)\n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._populate_tree()\n            self.set_status(f\"Added: {key}\")\n            self._close_dialog(dialog)\n        \n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(pady=10)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=lambda: self._close_dialog(dialog)).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Center dialog\n        dialog.update_idletasks()\n        x = self.winfo_rootx() + (self.winfo_width() - dialog.winfo_width()) // 2\n        y = self.winfo_rooty() + (self.winfo_height() - dialog.winfo_height()) // 2\n        dialog.geometry(f\"+{x}+{y}\")\n    \n    def _close_dialog(self, dialog):\n        \"\"\"Close dialog and reset flag.\"\"\"\n        self._dialog_open = False\n        dialog.destroy()\n    \n    def _delete_selected(self):\n        \"\"\"Delete selected row(s).\"\"\"\n        # Prevent concurrent delete operations\n        if self._delete_in_progress:\n            return\n        self._delete_in_progress = True\n        \n        try:\n            selection = self.tree.selection()\n            if not selection:\n                messagebox.showwarning(\"No Selection\", \"Please select a row to delete\")\n                return\n            \n            if messagebox.askyesno(\"Confirm\", \"Delete selected row(s)?\"):\n                deleted_count = 0\n                for item_id in selection:\n                    values = self.tree.item(item_id, 'values')\n                    key = values[0]\n                    \n                    # Remove from entries - only delete if key exists\n                    original_len = len(self.entries)\n                    self.entries = [e for e in self.entries if e.key != key]\n                    if len(self.entries) < original_len:\n                        deleted_count += 1\n                \n                if deleted_count > 0:\n                    self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n                    self.mark_dirty(True)\n                    self._populate_tree()\n                    self.set_status(f\"Deleted {deleted_count} row(s)\")\n        finally:\n            self._delete_in_progress = False\n    \n    def _edit_selected(self):\n        \"\"\"Edit selected row.\"\"\"\n        if self._dialog_open:\n            return\n        self._dialog_open = True\n        \n        selection = self.tree.selection()\n        if not selection:\n            self._dialog_open = False\n            return\n        \n        item_id = selection[0]\n        values = self.tree.item(item_id, 'values')\n        old_key = values[0]\n        old_value = values[1]\n        old_export = values[2] == '\u2713'\n        \n        # Find entry\n        entry = next((e for e in self.entries if e.key == old_key), None)\n        if not entry:\n            self._dialog_open = False\n            return\n        \n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"Edit Entry\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        dialog.protocol(\"WM_DELETE_WINDOW\", lambda: self._close_dialog(dialog))\n        \n        # Key field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Key:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        key_var = tk.StringVar(value=old_key)\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=key_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Value field\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Value:\").pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=2)\n        value_var = tk.StringVar(value=old_value)\n        ttk.Entry(dialog, textvariable=value_var, width=40).pack(padx=10, pady=2)\n        \n        # Export checkbox\n        export_var = tk.BooleanVar(value=old_export)\n        ttk.Checkbutton(dialog, text=\"Export (bash)\", variable=export_var).pack(anchor=tk.W, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            new_key = key_var.get().strip()\n            new_value = value_var.get().strip()\n            \n            if not new_key:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Key is required\")\n                return\n            \n            # Check if key changed and new key exists\n            if new_key != old_key and any(e.key == new_key for e in self.entries):\n                messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Key '{new_key}' already exists\")\n                return\n            \n            # Update entry\n            entry.key = new_key\n            entry.value = new_value\n            entry.is_export = export_var.get()\n            \n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._on_filter_changed()\n            self.set_status(f\"Updated: {new_key}\")\n            self._close_dialog(dialog)\n        \n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(pady=10)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=lambda: self._close_dialog(dialog)).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Center dialog\n        dialog.update_idletasks()\n        x = self.winfo_rootx() + (self.winfo_width() - dialog.winfo_width()) // 2\n        y = self.winfo_rooty() + (self.winfo_height() - dialog.winfo_height()) // 2\n        dialog.geometry(f\"+{x}+{y}\")\n    \n    def _import_file(self):\n        \"\"\"Import from another file.\"\"\"\n        filepath = filedialog.askopenfilename(\n            title=\"Import Key-Value File\",\n            filetypes=[(\"All Files\", \"*.*\"), (\"Env Files\", \"*.env\"), (\"Config\", \"*.conf\")]\n        )\n        if not filepath:\n            return\n        \n        try:\n            new_parser = GenericKVParser()\n            new_entries = new_parser.parse_file(filepath)\n            \n            # Merge or replace\n            if messagebox.askyesno(\"Import\", \"Replace current entries?\"):\n                self.entries = new_entries\n            else:\n                # Merge, skipping duplicates\n                existing_keys = {e.key for e in self.entries}\n                for entry in new_entries:\n                    if entry.key not in existing_keys:\n                        self.entries.append(entry)\n            \n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._populate_tree()\n            self.set_status(f\"Imported {len(new_entries)} entries from {filepath}\")\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Import Error\", str(e))\n    \n    def _export_file(self):\n        \"\"\"Export to another file.\"\"\"\n        filepath = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(\n            title=\"Export Key-Value File\",\n            defaultextension=\".env\",\n            filetypes=[(\"Env File\", \"*.env\"), (\"Config\", \"*.conf\"), (\"All\", \"*.*\")]\n        )\n        if not filepath:\n            return\n        \n        try:\n            # Update parser entries\n            self.parser.entries = self.entries\n            self.parser.write_back(filepath)\n            self.set_status(f\"Exported to {filepath}\")\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Export Error\", str(e))\n    \n    # Required abstract methods\n    \n    def load_data(self, data: str):\n        \"\"\"Load key-value content.\"\"\"\n        self.entries = self.parser.parse(data)\n        self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        self._original_data = data\n        self._populate_tree()\n        self.mark_dirty(False)\n        self.set_status(f\"Loaded {len(self.entries)} entries\")\n    \n    def get_data(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get key-value content.\"\"\"\n        self.parser.entries = self.entries\n        return self.parser.write_back()\n    \n    def validate(self) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n        \"\"\"Validate key-value data.\"\"\"\n        if not self.entries:\n            return True, \"\"  # Empty is valid\n        \n        # Check for duplicate keys\n        keys = [e.key for e in self.entries]\n        if len(keys) != len(set(keys)):\n            return False, \"Duplicate keys found\"\n        \n        # Check for invalid key names\n        for entry in self.entries:\n            if not entry.key:\n                return False, \"Empty key found\"\n            if ' ' in entry.key:\n                return False, f\"Key contains space: {entry.key}\"\n        \n        return True, \"\"\n</contentOfFile>\n</WriteFile>", "sessionId": 327, "rowId": 1, "timestamp": 1784290241.1226869, "date": "2026-07-17", "thinking": "", "prompt_tokens": 52503, "response_tokens": 3467} -->

Filter frame\n        filter_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        filter_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        ttk.Label(filter_frame, text=\"Filter:\").pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        self.filter_var = tk.StringVar()\n        self.filter_var.trace('w', self._on_filter_changed)\n        ttk.Entry(filter_frame, textvariable=self.filter_var, width=30).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(filter_frame, text=\"Clear\", command=self._clear_filter).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Buttons\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Add Resource\", command=self._add_resource).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Delete Selected\", command=self._delete_selected).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Insert Preset\", command=self._show_preset_picker).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # User presets button\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"My Presets\", command=self._manage_user_presets).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # XTerm helper buttons\n        ttk.Separator(btn_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL).pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.Y, padx=10)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"New XTerm\", command=self._launch_new_xterm).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"XTerm Tips\", command=self._show_xterm_tips).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Apply button (reloads X resources)\n        self.apply_btn = ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Apply (xrdb)\", command=self._apply_resources, \n                                    state=tk.DISABLED)\n        self.apply_btn.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Info label about xterm restart\n        info_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        info_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=5, pady=2)\n        self.info_label = ttk.Label(info_frame, text=\"\ud83d\udca1 Tip: xterm needs restart to see changes. Use 'New XTerm' or close/reopen.\", \n                                   foreground=\"gray\", font=('Helvetica', 9, 'italic'))\n        self.info_label.pack(side=tk.LEFT)\n        \n        # Bindings\n        self.tree.bind('<Double-1>', self._on_double_click)\n    \n    def _detect_resource_type(self, resource_path: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Detect resource type from resource path name for intelligent suggestions.\n        \n        Args:\n            resource_path: Resource path like 'XTerm*background', '*.color0'\n        \n        Returns:\n            'color', 'font', 'boolean', 'number', or 'generic'\n        \"\"\"\n        if not resource_path:\n            return 'generic'\n        \n        path_lower = resource_path.lower()\n        \n        # Color patterns\n        color_patterns = ['color', 'background', 'foreground', 'cursorcolor', \n                       'bordercolor', 'highlightcolor', 'troughcolor']\n        if any(p in path_lower for p in color_patterns):\n            return 'color'\n        \n        # Font patterns\n        font_patterns = ['font', 'face', 'facename']\n        if any(p in path_lower for p in font_patterns):\n            return 'font'\n        \n        # Boolean patterns\n        bool_patterns = ['shell', 'video', 'scroll', 'bell', 'bold', 'allow', \n                        'blink', 'underline', 'active', 'enabled', 'visible',\n                        'reverse', 'iconic', 'hold', 'utmp']\n        if any(p in path_lower for p in bool_patterns):\n            return 'boolean'\n        \n        # Number patterns\n        num_patterns = ['lines', 'chars', 'pixels', 'width', 'height', 'size',\n                       'borderwidth', 'margin', 'padding', 'timeout', 'interval']\n        if any(p in path_lower for p in num_patterns):\n            return 'number'\n        \n        return 'generic'\n    \n    def _launch_new_xterm(self):\n        \"\"\"Launch a new xterm instance with current XResources.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            # First apply current resources\n            if self.filepath and os.path.exists(self.filepath):\n                subprocess.run(['xrdb', '-merge', self.filepath], check=True, capture_output=True)\n            \n            # Launch xterm in background\n            subprocess.Popen(['xterm'], stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL, stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL)\n            self.set_status(\"\u2713 Launched new xterm with current resources\")\n            \n        except FileNotFoundError:\n            # Try uxterm as fallback\n            try:\n                subprocess.Popen(['uxterm'], stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL, stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL)\n                self.set_status(\"\u2713 Launched new uxterm with current resources\")\n            except FileNotFoundError:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"xterm Not Found\", \n                                   \"Neither 'xterm' nor 'uxterm' found.\\n\\n\"\n                                   \"Install xterm: sudo apt-get install xterm\")\n        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Failed to apply resources: {e}\")\n    \n    def _show_xterm_tips(self):\n        \"\"\"Show dialog explaining xterm restart behavior.\"\"\"\n        tips_text = \"\"\"XTerm Resource Loading - How It Works\n\nWhy don't my changes appear immediately?\n\n1. xrdb -merge loads resources into the X server\n2. Running xterm instances keep their OLD resources\n3. Only NEW xterm windows see the changes\n\nSolutions:\n\n\u2713 Use \"New XTerm\" button\n  - Applies resources then launches fresh xterm\n  - New window sees all changes immediately\n\n\u2713 Close and reopen xterm\n  - Old window keeps old colors/fonts\n  - New window loads fresh resources\n\n\u2713 Start xterm with specific file\n  - xterm -xrm \"*background: #ffffff\"\n\nCommon White Colors for xterm:\n\n  XTerm*background: #ffffff    (pure white)\n  XTerm*foreground: #000000    (black text)\n  XTerm*background: #f0f0f0    (off-white)\n  XTerm*foreground: #ffffff    (white text)\n\nRemember: Save \u2192 Apply \u2192 New XTerm to see changes!\"\"\"\n        \n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"XTerm Tips\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.geometry(\"500x450\")\n        \n        text = tk.Text(dialog, wrap=tk.WORD, padx=10, pady=10, font=('Courier', 10))\n        text.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)\n        text.insert('1.0', tips_text)\n        text.config(state=tk.DISABLED)\n        \n        ttk.Button(dialog, text=\"Close\", command=dialog.destroy).pack(pady=5)\n    \n    def _get_value_type(self, value: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Determine value type from value string.\"\"\"\n        value = value.strip().lower()\n        \n        if self.COLOR_HEX_PATTERN.match(value) or self.COLOR_RGB_PATTERN.match(value):\n            return 'color'\n        if value in ['true', 'false', 'yes', 'no', 'on', 'off']:\n            return 'boolean'\n        if 'font' in value or value.startswith('xft:') or value.startswith('-*-'):\n            return 'font'\n        \n        try:\n            int(value)\n            return 'number'\n        except ValueError:\n            try:\n                float(value)\n                return 'number'\n            except ValueError:\n                pass\n        \n        return 'string'\n    \n    def _get_color_preview(self, value: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get color for preview.\"\"\"\n        if self.COLOR_HEX_PATTERN.match(value):\n            return value\n        return ''\n    \n    def _populate_tree(self):\n        \"\"\"Populate treeview with entries.\"\"\"\n        # Clear existing\n        for item in self.tree.get_children():\n            self.tree.delete(item)\n        \n        # Add filtered entries\n        for entry in self.filtered_entries:\n            value_type = self._get_value_type(entry.value)\n            preview = self._get_color_preview(entry.value) if value_type == 'color' else ''\n            \n            item_id = self.tree.insert('', 'end', values=(\n                entry.resource_path,\n                entry.value,\n                value_type,\n                preview\n            ))\n            \n            # Set tag for color background\n            if preview:\n                self.tree.item(item_id, tags=(preview,))\n                self.tree.tag_configure(preview, background=preview)\n    \n    def _on_filter_changed(self, *args):\n        \"\"\"Apply filter.\"\"\"\n        filter_text = self.filter_var.get().lower()\n        \n        if not filter_text:\n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        else:\n            self.filtered_entries = [\n                e for e in self.entries \n                if filter_text in e.resource_path.lower() or filter_text in e.value.lower()\n            ]\n        \n        self._populate_tree()\n    \n    def _clear_filter(self):\n        \"\"\"Clear filter.\"\"\"\n        self.filter_var.set('')\n        self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        self._populate_tree()\n    \n    def _on_double_click(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Handle double click for editing with intelligent type detection.\"\"\"\n        selection = self.tree.selection()\n        if not selection:\n            return\n        \n        item = selection[0]\n        values = self.tree.item(item, 'values')\n        if not values:\n            return\n        \n        resource_path, current_value, value_type, _ = values\n        \n        # Use intelligent detection based on resource name\n        detected_type = self._detect_resource_type(resource_path)\n        \n        # Override with detected type if it's more specific\n        if detected_type == 'color' or value_type == 'color':\n            self._edit_color_with_presets(resource_path, current_value)\n        elif detected_type == 'font':\n            self._edit_with_presets(resource_path, current_value, 'font')\n        elif detected_type == 'boolean':\n            self._edit_with_presets(resource_path, current_value, 'boolean')\n        else:\n            self._edit_generic(resource_path, current_value)\n    \n    def _edit_color_with_presets(self, resource_path: str, current_value: str):\n        \"\"\"Edit color with color picker and preset dialog.geometry(\"400x550\")\n        \n        # Current value display\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Current Value:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=5)\n        current_var = match:\n                    r, g, b = match.groups()\n                    initial = f\"#{r[:2]}{g[:2]}{b[:2]}\"\n            \n            color = colorchooser.askcolor(initialcolor=initial, title=\"Choose Color\")\n            if color and color[1]:\n                current_var.set(color[1])\n                preview_label.config(bg=color[1])\n        \n        ttk.Button(dialog, text=\"\ud83c\udfa8 Pick Color...\", command=pick_color).pack(pady=5)\n        \n        # Preset colors\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Quick Presets:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=5)\n        \n        preset_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        preset_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        # Show common colors in a grid\n ('Cyan', '#00ffff'), ('Magenta', '#ff00ff'),\n            ('Gray', '#808080'), ('Orange', '#ffa500'),\n        ]\n        \n        for i, (name, color) in enumerate(common_colors):\n            btn = preview_label.config(bg=c)))\n            btn.grid(row=i//5, column=i%5, padx=2, pady=2)\n        \n        # Terminal colors\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Terminal Colors:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=5)\n        \n        term_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        term_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        for i in range(8):\n            color_val = XTERM_COLORS[f'color{i}']\n            btn = tk.Button(term_frame, text=f\"color{i}\", bg=color_val, \n                          fg='white' if i in [0, 4] else 'black',\n                          width=8, command=lambda c=color_val: (current_var.set(c), preview_label.config(bg=c)))\n            btn.grid(row=0, column=i, padx=2, pady=2)\n        \n        # Save as preset button\n        def save_as_preset():\n            name = simpledialog.askstring(\"Save Preset\", \"Enter preset name:\", parent=dialog)\n            if name:\n                if add_user_preset(name, current_var.get()):\n                    messagebox.showinfo(\"Success\", f\"Saved '{name}' to My Presets\", parent=dialog)\n                else:\n                    messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Failed to save preset\", parent=dialog)\n        \n        ttk.Button(dialog, text=\"\u2b50 Save as Preset\", command=save_as_preset).pack(pady=10)\n        \n        # Buttons\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=10)\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            self._update_entry(resource_path, current_var.get())\n            dialog.destroy()\n        \n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=dialog.destroy).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)\n    \n    def _edit_with_presets(self, resource_path: str, current_value: str, preset_type: str):\n        \"\"\"Edit with preset dropdown for fonts, booleans, etc.\"\"\"\n        dialog = new_value: str):\n        \"\"\"Update an entry value.\"\"\"\n        # Update in parser\n        if self.parser.update_value(resource_path, new_value):\n            # Update in our list\n            for entry in self.entries:\n                if entry.resource_path == resource_path:\n                    entry.value = new_value\n                    break\n            \n            self.mark_dirty(True)\n            self._on_filter_changed()  # Refresh display\n            self.set_status(f\"Updated {resource_path}\")\n    \n    def _manage_user_presets(self):\n   preset_tree.bind('<Double-1>', lambda e: on_select())\n        \n        self.wait_window(dialog)\n        \n        # Apply result if any\n        if result['value']:\n            selection = category):\n        \"\"\"Load presets into treeview.\"\"\"\n        # Clear existing\n        for item in tree.get_children():\n            tree.delete(item)\n        \n        presets = get_all_presets()\n        \n        if category in presets:\n            for name, value in presets[category]['items']:\n                tree.insert('', 'end', values=(name, value))\n    \n    def _filter_presets(self, tree, category, search_text):\n        \"\"\"Filter presets by search text.\"\"\"\n        # Clear and reload\n        for item in tree.get_children():\n            tree.delete(item)\n        \n        presets = get_all_presets()\n        search_lower = search_text.lower()\n        \n        if category in presets:\n            for name, value in presets[category]['items']:\n                if not search_text or search_lower in name.lower() or search_lower in str(value).lower():\n                    tree.insert('', 'end', values=(name, value))\n    \n    def _add_preset_as_new(self, value):\n        \"\"\"Add a new resource with preset value.\"\"\"\n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"New Resource with <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nXResources Editor Widget for KosXER\n\nTreeview-based editor for .Xresources and .Xdefaults files.\nIncludes Apply button to reload resources with xrdb, preset picker, and user presets.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk, colorchooser, messagebox, simpledialog\nimport re\nimport subprocess\nimport os\nfrom typing import Optional, List\n\nfrom gui.editor_base import EditorWidget\nfrom parsers.xresources_parser import XResourcesParser, XResourceEntry\nfrom config.presets import (\n    get_presets_for_resource, get_all_presets, XTERM_COLORS,\n    add_user_preset, delete_user_preset, get_user_presets_list,\n    load_user_presets, USER_PRESETS_FILE\n)\n\n\nclass XResourcesEditor(EditorWidget):\n    \"\"\"Editor widget for XResources files.\"\"\"\n    \n    COLOR_HEX_PATTERN = re.compile(r'^#[0-9a-fA-F]{6}$')\n    COLOR_RGB_PATTERN = re.compile(r'^rgb:([0-9a-fA-F]{2,4})/([0-9a-fA-F]{2,4})/([0-9a-fA-F]{2,4})$')\n    \n    def __init__(self, parent, main_window=None, filepath: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs):\n        self.parser = XResourcesParser()\n        self.entries: List[XResourceEntry] = []\n        self.filtered_entries: List[XResourceEntry] = []\n        super().__init__(parent, main_window, filepath, **kwargs)\n    \n    def __init__(self, parent, main_window=None, filepath: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs):\n        self.parser = XResourcesParser()\n        self.entries: List[XResourceEntry] = []\n        self.filtered_entries: List[XResourceEntry] = []\n        self._dialog_open = False  # Prevent duplicate dialogs\n        self._delete_in_progress = False  # Prevent duplicate deletes\n        super().__init__(parent, main_window, filepath, **kwargs)\n        \n        ttk.Label(filter_frame, text=\"Filter:\").pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        self.filter_var = tk.StringVar()\n        self.filter_var.trace('w', self._on_filter_changed)\n        ttk.Entry(filter_frame, textvariable=self.filter_var, width=30).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(filter_frame, text=\"Clear\", command=self._clear_filter).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Treeview\n        tree_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        tree_frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, pady=5)\n        \n        columns = ('resource', 'value', 'type', 'preview')\n        self.tree = ttk.Treeview(tree_frame, columns=columns, show='headings')\n        \n        self.tree.heading('resource', text='Resource Path')\n        self.tree.heading('value', text='Value')\n        self.tree.heading('type', text='Type')\n        self.tree.heading('preview', text='Preview')\n        \n        self.tree.column('resource', width=300)\n        self.tree.column('value', width=250)\n        self.tree.column('type', width=100)\n        self.tree.column('preview', width=50)\n        \n        y_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.tree.yview)\n        x_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.tree.xview)\n        self.tree.configure(yscrollcommand=y_scroll.set, xscrollcommand=x_scroll.set)\n        \n        y_scroll.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)\n        x_scroll.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)\n        self.tree.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)\n        \n        # Buttons\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Add Resource\", command=self._add_resource).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Delete Selected\", command=self._delete_selected).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Insert Preset\", command=self._show_preset_picker).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # User presets button\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"My Presets\", command=self._manage_user_presets).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # XTerm helper buttons\n        ttk.Separator(btn_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL).pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.Y, padx=10)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"New XTerm\", command=self._launch_new_xterm).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"XTerm Tips\", command=self._show_xterm_tips).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Apply button (reloads X resources)\n        self.apply_btn = ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Apply (xrdb)\", command=self._apply_resources, \n                                    state=tk.DISABLED)\n        self.apply_btn.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Info label about xterm restart\n        info_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        info_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=5, pady=2)\n        self.info_label = ttk.Label(info_frame, text=\"\ud83d\udca1 Tip: xterm needs restart to see changes. Use 'New XTerm' or close/reopen.\", \n                                   foreground=\"gray\", font=('Helvetica', 9, 'italic'))\n        self.info_label.pack(side=tk.LEFT)\n        \n        # Bindings\n        self.tree.bind('<Double-1>', self._on_double_click)\n    \n    def _detect_resource_type(self, resource_path: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Detect resource type from resource path name for intelligent suggestions.\n        \n        Args:\n            resource_path: Resource path like 'XTerm*background', '*.color0'\n        \n        Returns:\n            'color', 'font', 'boolean', 'number', or 'generic'\n        \"\"\"\n        if not resource_path:\n            return 'generic'\n        \n        path_lower = resource_path.lower()\n        \n        # Color patterns\n        color_patterns = ['color', 'background', 'foreground', 'cursorcolor', \n                       'bordercolor', 'highlightcolor', 'troughcolor']\n        if any(p in path_lower for p in color_patterns):\n            return 'color'\n        \n        # Font patterns\n        font_patterns = ['font', 'face', 'facename']\n        if any(p in path_lower for p in font_patterns):\n            return 'font'\n        \n        # Boolean patterns\n        bool_patterns = ['shell', 'video', 'scroll', 'bell', 'bold', 'allow', \n                        'blink', 'underline', 'active', 'enabled', 'visible',\n                        'reverse', 'iconic', 'hold', 'utmp']\n        if any(p in path_lower for p in bool_patterns):\n            return 'boolean'\n        \n        # Number patterns\n        num_patterns = ['lines', 'chars', 'pixels', 'width', 'height', 'size',\n                       'borderwidth', 'margin', 'padding', 'timeout', 'interval']\n        if any(p in path_lower for p in num_patterns):\n            return 'number'\n        \n        return 'generic'\n    \n    def _launch_new_xterm(self):\n        \"\"\"Launch a new xterm instance with current XResources.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            # First apply current resources\n            if self.filepath and os.path.exists(self.filepath):\n                subprocess.run(['xrdb', '-merge', self.filepath], check=True, capture_output=True)\n            \n            # Launch xterm in background\n            subprocess.Popen(['xterm'], stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL, stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL)\n            self.set_status(\"\u2713 Launched new xterm with current resources\")\n            \n        except FileNotFoundError:\n            # Try uxterm as fallback\n            try:\n                subprocess.Popen(['uxterm'], stdout=subprocess.DEVNULL, stderr=subprocess.DEVNULL)\n                self.set_status(\"\u2713 Launched new uxterm with current resources\")\n            except FileNotFoundError:\n                messagebox.showerror(\"xterm Not Found\", \n                                   \"Neither 'xterm' nor 'uxterm' found.\\n\\n\"\n                                   \"Install xterm: sudo apt-get install xterm\")\n        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Failed to apply resources: {e}\")\n    \n    def _show_xterm_tips(self):\n        \"\"\"Show dialog explaining xterm restart behavior.\"\"\"\n        tips_text = \"\"\"XTerm Resource Loading - How It Works\n\nWhy don't my changes appear immediately?\n\n1. xrdb -merge loads resources into the X server\n2. Running xterm instances keep their OLD resources\n3. Only NEW xterm windows see the changes\n\nSolutions:\n\n\u2713 Use \"New XTerm\" button\n  - Applies resources then launches fresh xterm\n  - New window sees all changes immediately\n\n\u2713 Close and reopen xterm\n  - Old window keeps old colors/fonts\n  - New window loads fresh resources\n\n\u2713 Start xterm with specific file\n  - xterm -xrm \"*background: #ffffff\"\n\nCommon White Colors for xterm:\n\n  XTerm*background: #ffffff    (pure white)\n  XTerm*foreground: #000000    (black text)\n  XTerm*background: #f0f0f0    (off-white)\n  XTerm*foreground: #ffffff    (white text)\n\nRemember: Save \u2192 Apply \u2192 New XTerm to see changes!\"\"\"\n        \n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(\"XTerm Tips\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.geometry(\"500x450\")\n        \n        text = tk.Text(dialog, wrap=tk.WORD, padx=10, pady=10, font=('Courier', 10))\n        text.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=5, pady=5)\n        text.insert('1.0', tips_text)\n        text.config(state=tk.DISABLED)\n        \n        ttk.Button(dialog, text=\"Close\", command=dialog.destroy).pack(pady=5)\n    \n    def _get_value_type(self, value: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Determine value type from value string.\"\"\"\n        value = value.strip().lower()\n        \n        if self.COLOR_HEX_PATTERN.match(value) or self.COLOR_RGB_PATTERN.match(value):\n            return 'color'\n        if value in ['true', 'false', 'yes', 'no', 'on', 'off']:\n            return 'boolean'\n        if 'font' in value or value.startswith('xft:') or value.startswith('-*-'):\n            return 'font'\n        \n        try:\n            int(value)\n            return 'number'\n        except ValueError:\n            try:\n                float(value)\n                return 'number'\n            except ValueError:\n                pass\n        \n        return 'string'\n    \n    def _get_color_preview(self, value: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get color for preview.\"\"\"\n        if self.COLOR_HEX_PATTERN.match(value):\n            return value\n        return ''\n    \n    def _populate_tree(self):\n        \"\"\"Populate treeview with entries.\"\"\"\n        # Clear existing\n        for item in self.tree.get_children():\n            self.tree.delete(item)\n        \n        # Add filtered entries\n        for entry in self.filtered_entries:\n            value_type = self._get_value_type(entry.value)\n            preview = self._get_color_preview(entry.value) if value_type == 'color' else ''\n            \n            item_id = self.tree.insert('', 'end', values=(\n                entry.resource_path,\n                entry.value,\n                value_type,\n                preview\n            ))\n            \n            # Set tag for color background\n            if preview:\n                self.tree.item(item_id, tags=(preview,))\n                self.tree.tag_configure(preview, background=preview)\n    \n    def _on_filter_changed(self, *args):\n        \"\"\"Apply filter.\"\"\"\n        filter_text = self.filter_var.get().lower()\n        \n        if not filter_text:\n            self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        else:\n            self.filtered_entries = [\n                e for e in self.entries \n                if filter_text in e.resource_path.lower() or filter_text in e.value.lower()\n            ]\n        \n        self._populate_tree()\n    \n    def _clear_filter(self):\n        \"\"\"Clear filter.\"\"\"\n        self.filter_var.set('')\n        self.filtered_entries = self.entries[:]\n        self._populate_tree()\n    \n    def _on_double_click(self, event):\n        \"\"\"Handle double click for editing with intelligent type detection.\"\"\"\n        selection = self.tree.selection()\n        if not selection:\n            return\n        \n        item = selection[0]\n        values = self.tree.item(item, 'values')\n        if not values:\n            return\n        \n        resource_path, current_value, value_type, _ = values\n        \n        # Use intelligent detection based on resource name\n        detected_type = self._detect_resource_type(resource_path)\n        \n        # Override with detected type if it's more specific\n        if detected_type == 'color' or value_type == 'color':\n            self._edit_color_with_presets(resource_path, current_value)\n        elif detected_type == 'font':\n            self._edit_with_presets(resource_path, current_value, 'font')\n        elif detected_type == 'boolean':\n            self._edit_with_presets(resource_path, current_value, 'boolean')\n        else:\n            self._edit_generic(resource_path, current_value)\n    \n    def _edit_color_with_presets(self, resource_path: str, current_value: str):\n        \"\"\"Edit color with color picker and preset colors.\"\"\"\n        dialog = tk.Toplevel(self)\n        dialog.title(f\"Edit Color - {resource_path}\")\n        dialog.transient(self)\n        dialog.grab_set()\n        dialog.geometry(\"400x550\")\n        \n        # Current value display\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Current Value:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=5)\n        current_var = ttk.Frame(dialog, width=100, height=50)\n        preview_frame.pack(pady=10)\n        preview_frame.pack_propagate(False)\n        \n        preview_label = tk.Label(preview_frame, text=\"Preview\", pick_color():\n            initial = current_var.get()\n            if self.COLOR_RGB_PATTERN.match(initial):\n                match = self.COLOR_RGB_PATTERN.match(initial)\n                if match:\n                    r, g, b = match.groups()\n                    initial = f\"#{r[:2]}{g[:2]}{b[:2]}\"\n            \n            color = colorchooser.askcolor(initialcolor=initial, title=\"Choose Color\")\n            if color and color[1]:\n                current_var.set(color[1])\n                preview_label.config(bg=color[1])\n        \n        ttk.Button(dialog, text=\"\ud83c\udfa8 Pick Color...\", command=pick_color).pack(pady=5)\n        \n        # Preset colors\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Quick Presets:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=5)\n        \n        preset_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        preset_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        # Show common colors in a grid\n        common_colors = [\n            ('White', '#ffffff'), ('Black', '#000000'),\n            ('Red', '#ff0000'), ('Green', '#00ff00'),\n            ('Blue', '#0000ff'), ('Yellow', '#ffff00'),\n            ('Cyan', '#00ffff'), ('Magenta', '#ff00ff'),\n            ('Gray', '#808080'), ('Orange', '#ffa500'),\n        ]\n        \n        for i, (name, color) in enumerate(common_colors):\n            btn = tk.Button(preset_frame, text=name, bg=color, fg='white' if color in ['#000000', '#0000ff', '#808080'] else 'black',\n                          width=8, command=lambda c=color: (current_var.set(c), preview_label.config(bg=c)))\n            btn.grid(row=i//5, column=i%5, padx=2, pady=2)\n        \n        # Terminal colors\n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Terminal Colors:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=5)\n        \n        term_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        term_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=5)\n        \n        for i in range(8):\n            color_val = width=8, command=lambda c=color_val: (current_var.set(c), preview_label.config(bg=c)))\n            btn.grid(row=0, column=i, padx=2, pady=2)\n        \n        # Save as preset button\n        def save_as_preset():\n            name = simpledialog.askstring(\"Save Preset\", \"Enter preset name:\", parent=dialog)\n            if name:\n                if add_user_preset(name, \"Failed to save preset\", parent=dialog)\n        \n        ttk.Button(dialog, text=\"\u2b50 Save as Preset\", command=save_as_preset).pack(pady=10)\n        \n        # Buttons\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=10)\n        \n        def on_ok():\n            self._update_entry(resource_path, current_var.get())\n            dialog.destroy()\n        \n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"OK\", command=on_ok).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Cancel\", command=dialog.destroy).pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=5)\n    \n    def _edit_with_presets(self, resource_path: str, current_value: str, preset_type: str):\n        \"\"\"Edit with preset dropdown for fonts, booleans, etc.\"\"\"\n        dialog = as Preset\", command=save_as_preset).pack(pady=10)\n        \n        # Buttons\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(dialog)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=10)\n        \n        def       dialog.geometry(\"400x250\")\n        \n        ttk.Label(dialog, text=\"Value:\", font=('Helvetica', 10, 'bold')).pack(pady=5)\n        current_var = tk.StringVar(value=current_value)\n #!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> Generic Key-Value Parser for KosXER
> 
> Handles simple KEY=value format files:
> - Bash-style exports (export KEY=value)

> - Application config files
> - .env files

> - Comments (#)
