<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nGeneric Key-Value Parser for KosXER\n\nHandles simple KEY=value format files:\n- Bash-style exports (export KEY=value)\n- Systemd environment files\n- Application config files\n- .env files\n\nFeatures:\n- Comments (#)\n- Empty lines\n- Quoted values (single/double quotes)\n- Escape sequences (\\\\n, \\\\t, etc.)\n- Line continuation with backslash\n\"\"\"\n\nimport re\nimport os\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Optional, Union, Any\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass KVEntry:\n    \"\"\"Represents a key-value entry.\"\"\"\n    key: str\n    value: str\n    comment: Optional[str] = None\n    line_number: int = 0\n    is_export: bool = False  # ings.cpython-314.pyc\n(cwd: <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nKey-Value Editor Widget for KosXER\n\nSimple two-column editor for KEY=value files.\nGood for .env files, simple configs, shell exports, etc.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport logging\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk, messagebox, filedialog\nfrom typing import Optional, List, Dict\n\nfrom gui.editor_base import EditorWidget\nfrom parsers.generic_kv_parser import GenericKVParser, KVEntry\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger('kosxer.kv_editor')\n\nclass KVEditor(EditorWidget):\n    \"\"\"\n    Editor widget for key-value configuration files.\n    \n    Features:\n    - Two-column editable treeview (Key, Value)\n    - Add/Delete rows\n    - Import/Export functionality\n    - Search/filter\n    - Intelligent quote handling\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, parent, main_window=None, filepath: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs):\n        self.parser = GenericKVParser()\n        self.entries: List[KVEntry] = []\n        self.filtered_entries: List[KVEntry] = []\n        self._edit_popup: Optional[tk.Toplevel] = None\n        self._dialog_open = False  # Prevent duplicate dialogs\n        self._delete_in_progress = False  # Prevent duplicate deletes\n        \n        super().__init__(parent, main_window, filepath, **kwargs)\n    \n    def _create_editor_widgets(self):\n        \"\"\"Create the KV editor UI.\"\"\"\n        # Filter frame\n        filter_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        filter_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        ttk.Label(filter_frame, text=\"Search:\").pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        self.filter_var = tk.StringVar()\n        self.filter_var.trace('w', self._on_filter_changed)\n        ttk.Entry(filter_frame, textvariable=self.filter_var, width=30).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        ttk.Button(filter_frame, text=\"Clear\", command=self._clear_filter).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Treeview frame\n        tree_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        tree_frame.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, pady=5)\n        \n        # Treeview\n        columns = ('key', 'value', 'export')\n        self.tree = ttk.Treeview(tree_frame, columns=columns, show='headings')\n        \n        self.tree.heading('key', text='Key')\n        self.tree.heading('value', text='Value')\n        self.tree.heading('export', text='Export')\n        \n        self.tree.column('key', width=200)\n        self.tree.column('value', width=400)\n        self.tree.column('export', width=60)\n        \n        # Scrollbars\n        y_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL, command=self.tree.yview)\n        x_scroll = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL, command=self.tree.xview)\n        self.tree.configure(yscrollcommand=y_scroll.set, xscrollcommand=x_scroll.set)\n        \n        y_scroll.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y)\n        x_scroll.pack(side=tk.BOTTOM, fill=tk.X)\n        self.tree.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True)\n        \n        # Button frame\n        btn_frame = ttk.Frame(self.editor_frame)\n        btn_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=5)\n        \n        # Row operations\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Add Row\", command=self._add_row).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Delete Selected\", command=self._delete_selected).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Edit Selected\", command=self._edit_selected).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        ttk.Separator(btn_frame, orient=tk.VERTICAL).pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.Y, padx=10)\n        \n        # Import/Export\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Import\", command=self._import_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        ttk.Button(btn_frame, text=\"Export\", command=self._export_file).pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)\n        \n        # Bindings\n        self.tree.bind('<Double-1>', self._on_double_click)\n        self.tree.bind('<Delete>', lambda e: self._delete_selected())\n        self.tree.bind('<Return>', lambda e: self._edit_selected())\n    \n    def _populate_tree(self):\n        \"\"\"Populate treeview with entries.\"\"\"\n        # #!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> Generic Key-Value Parser for KosXER
> 
> Handles simple KEY=value format files:
> - Bash-style exports (export KEY=value)
> - Systemd environment files
> - Application config files
> - .env files
> 
> Features:
> - Comments (#)
> - Empty lines
> - Quoted values (single/double quotes)
> - Escape sequences (\\n, \\t, etc.)
> - Line continuation with backslash
> """

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nGeneric Key-Value Parser for KosXER\n\nHandles simple KEY=value format files:\n- Bash-style exports (export KEY=value)\n- Systemd environment files\n- Application config files\n- .env files\n\nFeatures:\n- Comments (#)\n- Empty lines\n- Quoted values (single/double quotes)\n- Escape sequences (\\\\n, \\\\t, etc.)\n- Line continuation with backslash\n\"\"\"\n\nimport re\nimport os\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Optional, Union, Any\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass KVEntry:\n    \"\"\"Represents a key-value entry.\"\"\"\n    key: str\n    value: str\n    comment: Optional[str] = None\n    line_number: int = 0\n    is_export: bool = False  # Whether it was defined with 'export'\n    raw_line: str = \"\"  # Original line\n    \n    def to_line(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Convert back to file line format.\"\"\"\n        export_prefix = \"export \" if self.is_export else \"\"\n        if self.comment:\n            return f\"{export_prefix}{self.key}={self.value}  # {self.comment}\"\n        return f\"{export_prefix}{self.key}={self.value}\"\n\n\nclass GenericKVParser:\n    \"\"\"\n    Parser for generic KEY=value configuration files.\n    \n    Supports:\n    - Simple KEY=value\n    - export KEY=value (bash-style)\n    - Comments (#)\n    - Quoted values\n    - Escape sequences\n    - Line continuation\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    # Patterns\n    COMMENT_PATTERN = re.compile(r'^\\s*#(.*)$')\n    EXPORT_PATTERN = re.compile(r'^\\s*export\\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)\\s*=\\s*(.*)$')\n    KV_PATTERN = re.compile(r'^([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_]*)\\s*=\\s*(.*)$')\n    WHITESPACE_PATTERN = re.compile(r'^\\s*$')\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.entries: List[KVEntry] = []\n        self._escape_map = {\n            '\\\\n': '\\n',\n            '\\\\t': '\\t',\n            '\\\\r': '\\r',\n            '\\\\\\\\': '\\\\',\n            '\\\\\"': '\"',\n            \"\\\\'\": \"'\",\n        }\n        \n    def parse(self, content: str) -> List[KVEntry]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse KEY=value content.\n        \n        Args:\n            content: File content to parse\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of KVEntry objects\n        \"\"\"\n        self.entries = []\n        lines = content.split('\\n')\n        pending_comment = None\n        i = 0\n        \n        while i < len(lines):\n            line = lines[i]\n            line_num = i + 1\n            \n            # Handle line continuation with backslash\n            while line.rstrip().endswith('\\\\') and i + 1 < len(lines):\n                line = line.rstrip()[:-1] + lines[i + 1]\n                i += 1\n            \n            stripped = line.strip()\n            \n            # Skip empty lines\n            if self.WHITESPACE_PATTERN.match(stripped):\n                pending_comment = None\n                i += 1\n                continue\n            \n            # Handle comments\n            if stripped.startswith('#'):\n                comment_text = stripped[1:].strip()\n                pending_comment = comment_text\n                i += 1\n                continue\n            \n            # Try export pattern first\n            export_match = self.EXPORT_PATTERN.match(line)\n            if export_match:\n                key = export_match.group(1)\n                value = self._unescape_value(self._unquote(export_match.group(2).strip()))\n                self._add_entry(key, value, pending_comment, line_num, line, is_export=True)\n                pending_comment = None\n                i += 1\n                continue\n            \n            # Try simple KEY=value\n            kv_match = self.KV_PATTERN.match(line)\n            if kv_match:\n                key = kv_match.group(1)\n                value = self._unescape_value(self._unquote(kv_match.group(2).strip()))\n                self._add_entry(key, value, pending_comment, line_num, line, is_export=False)\n                pending_comment = None\n                i += 1\n                continue\n            \n            i += 1\n        \n        return self.entries\n    \n    def _add_entry(self, key: str, value: str, comment: Optional[str],\n                   line_number: int, raw_line: str, is_export: bool = False):\n        \"\"\"Add a new entry.\"\"\"\n        entry = KVEntry(\n            key=key,\n            value=value,\n            comment=comment,\n            line_number=line_number,\n            is_export=is_export,\n            raw_line=raw_line\n        )\n        self.entries.append(entry)\n    \n    def _unquote(self, value: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Remove quotes from value.\"\"\"\n        if len(value) >= 2:\n            # Double quotes\n            if value[0] == '\"' and value[-1] == '\"':\n                return value[1:-1]\n            # Single quotes\n            if value[0] == \"'\" and value[-1] == \"'\":\n                return value[1:-1]\n        return value\n    \n    def _unescape_value(self, value: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Process escape sequences.\"\"\"\n        result = []\n        i = 0\n        while i < len(value):\n            if value[i] == '\\\\' and i + 1 < len(value):\n                escape = value[i:i+2]\n                if escape in self._escape_map:\n                    result.append(self._escape_map[escape])\n                    i += 2\n                    continue\n            result.append(value[i])\n            i += 1\n        return ''.join(result)\n    \n    def _escape_value(self, value: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Escape special characters for writing back.\"\"\"\n        # Reverse the escape map\n        reverse_map = {v: k for k, v in self._escape_map.items()}\n        result = value\n        for char, esc in reverse_map.items():\n            result = result.replace(char, esc)\n        return result\n    \n    def parse_file(self, filepath: Union[str, Path]) -> List[KVEntry]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse a file from disk.\n        \n        Args:\n            filepath: Path to file\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of KVEntry objects\n        \"\"\"\n        filepath = Path(filepath)\n        \n        if not filepath.exists():\n            raise FileNotFoundError(f\"File not found: {filepath}\")\n        \n        with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n            content = f.read()\n        \n        return self.parse(content)\n    \n    def get(self, key: str, default: Any = None) -> Any:\n        \"\"\"Get value by key.\"\"\"\n        for entry in self.entries:\n            if entry.key == key:\n                return entry.value\n        return default\n    \n    def set(self, key: str, value: str, is_export: bool = False):\n        \"\"\"Set or add a key-value pair.\"\"\"\n        for entry in self.entries:\n            if entry.key == key:\n                entry.value = value\n                entry.is_export = is_export\n                return\n        # Add new\n        self.entries.append(KVEntry(key=key, value=value, is_export=is_export))\n    \n    def remove(self, key: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Remove an entry by key.\"\"\"\n        for i, entry in enumerate(self.entries):\n            if entry.key == key:\n                self.entries.pop(i)\n                return True\n        return False\n    \n    def write_back(self, filepath: Optional[Union[str, Path]] = None) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate file content from entries.\n        \n        Args:\n            filepath: Optional path to write to\n            \n        Returns:\n            File content as string\n        \"\"\"\n        lines = []\n        \n        for entry in self.entries:\n            # Quote if contains spaces\n            if ' ' in escaped_value and not (escaped_value.startswith('\"') or escaped_value.startswith(\"'\")):\n                escaped_value = f'\"{escaped_value}\"'\n            lines.append(f\"{export_prefix}{entry.key}={escaped_value}\")\n        \n        content = '\\n'.join(lines)\n        \n        if filepath:\n            filepath = Path(filepath)\n            with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                f.write(content)\n        \n        return content\n    \n    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, str]:\n        \"\"\"Convert entries to dictionary.\"\"\"\n        return {entry.key: entry.value for entry in self.entries}\n    \n    def from_dict(self, data: Dict[str, str], is_export: bool = False):\n        \"\"\"Load from dictionary.\"\"\"\n        self.entries = []\n        for key, value in data.items():\n            self.entries.append(KVEntry(key=key, value=value, is_export=is_export))\n    \n    def __len__(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Return number of entries.\"\"\"\n        return len(self.entries)\n    \n    def __iter__(self):\n        \"\"\"Iterate over entries.\"\"\"\n        return iter(self.entries)\n    \n    def __contains__(self, key: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if key exists.\"\"\"\n        return any(entry.key == key for entry in self.entries)\n\n\n# Convenience functions\n\ndef parse_env_file(filepath: Union[str, Path]) -> Dict[str, str]:\n    \"\"\"Parse a .env file and return dictionary.\"\"\"\n    parser = GenericKVParser()\n    parser.parse_file(filepath)\n    return parser.to_dict()\n\n\ndef parse_exports(content: str) -> Dict[str, str]:\n    \"\"\"Parse bash export statements.\"\"\"\n    parser = GenericKVParser()\n    parser.parse(content)\n    return parser.to_dict()\n", "sessionId": 327, "rowId": 3, "timestamp": 1784290572.1441581, "date": "2026-07-17", "name": "ReadFile"} -->

#!/usr/bin/env python3
> """
> AUTOVERSION - Single Source of Truth for KosXER Version
> 
> This file defines the VERSION constant and provides functions
> to increment it automatically on git commits.
> 
> Usage as module:
>     from AUTOVERSION import VERSION
>     print(f"App version: {VERSION}")
> 
> Usage as script:
>     python AUTOVERSION.py          # Increment version
>     python AUTOVERSION.py --show   # Show current version
> """
> 
> import sys
> import re
> import os
> from pathlib import Path

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nAUTOVERSION - Single Source of Truth for KosXER Version\n\nThis file defines the VERSION constant and provides functions\nto increment it automatically on git commits.\n\nUsage as module:\n    from AUTOVERSION import VERSION\n    print(f\"App version: {VERSION}\")\n\nUsage as script:\n    python AUTOVERSION.py          # Increment version\n    python AUTOVERSION.py --show   # Show current version\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport re\nimport os\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\n# =============================================================================\n# VERSION - Single Source of Truth\n# =============================================================================\nVERSION = \"1.0.1\"\n\n# Version file location (relative to this file)\nVERSION_FILE = Path(__file__).parent / \"config\" / \"VERSION\"\n\n\ndef parse_version(version_str: str) -> tuple:\n    \"\"\"Parse version string into tuple (major, minor, patch).\"\"\"\n    parts = version_str.split('.')\n    major = int(parts[0]) if len(parts) > 0 else 1\n    minor = int(parts[1]) if len(parts) > 1 else 0\n    patch = int(parts[2]) if len(parts) > 2 else 0\n    return (major, minor, patch)\n\n\ndef format_version(major: int, minor: int, patch: int) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Format version tuple into string.\"\"\"\n    return f\"{major}.{minor}.{patch}\"\n\n\ndef increment_version(version_str: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"\n    Increment version number (patch level).\n    \n    Examples:\n        \"1.0\"     -> \"1.0.1\"\n        \"1.0.0\"   -> \"1.0.1\"\n        \"1.0.9\"   -> \"1.0.10\"\n        \"1.2.99\"  -> \"1.2.100\"\n    \"\"\"\n    major, minor, patch = parse_version(version_str)\n    \n    if len(version_str.split('.')) == 2:\n        # Was X.Y format, start patch at 1\n        return format_version(major, minor, 1)\n    else:\n        # Increment patch\n        return format_version(major, minor, patch + 1)\n\n\ndef update_version_file(new_version: str):\n    \"\"\"Update the VERSION constant in this file.\"\"\"\n    this_file = Path(__file__)\n    \n    try:\n        content = this_file.read_text()\n        \n        # Replace VERSION = \"X.Y.Z\" with new version\n        new_content = re.sub(\n            r'^(VERSION\\s*=\\s*[\"\\'])([\\d.]+)([\"\\'])',\n            rf'\\g<1>{new_version}\\g<3>',\n            content,\n            flags=re.MULTILINE\n        )\n        \n        if new_content != content:\n            this_file.write_text(new_content)\n            print(f\"Updated AUTOVERSION.py: {new_version}\")\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error updating AUTOVERSION.py: {e}\", file=sys.stderr)\n\n\ndef update_constants_py(new_version: str):\n    \"\"\"Update version in config/constants.py.\"\"\"\n    constants_file = Path(__file__).parent / \"config\" / \"constants.py\"\n    \n    if not constants_file.exists():\n        return\n    \n    try:\n        content = constants_file.read_text()\n        \n        # Update VERSION constant\n        new_content = re.sub(\n            r'^(VERSION\\s*=\\s*[\"\\'])([\\d.]+)([\"\\'])',\n            rf'\\g<1>{new_version}\\g<3>',\n            content,\n            flags=re.MULTILINE\n        )\n        \n        if new_content != content:\n            constants_file.write_text(new_content)\n            print(f\"Updated config/constants.py: {new_version}\")\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error updating constants.py: {e}\", file=sys.stderr)\n\n\ndef update_version_file_txt(new_version: str):\n    \"\"\"Update plain text VERSION file.\"\"\"\n    version_file = Path(__file__).parent / \"config\" / \"VERSION\"\n    \n    try:\n        version_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n        version_file.write_text(new_version + '\\n')\n        print(f\"Updated config/VERSION: {new_version}\")\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"Error writing VERSION file: {e}\", file=sys.stderr)\n\n\ndef show_version():\n    \"\"\"Display current version.\"\"\"\n    print(f\"KosXER version: {VERSION}\")\n    print(f\"Version file: {VERSION_FILE}\")\n\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Main entry point for auto-versioning.\"\"\"\n    # Check for --show flag\n    if len(sys.argv) > 1 and sys.argv[1] in ('--show', '-s', 'show'):\n        show_version()\n        return 0\n    \n    # Increment version\n    current = VERSION\n    new_version = increment_version(current)\n    \n    print(f\"Incrementing version: {current} -> {new_version}\")\n    \n    # Update all version files\n    update_version_file(new_version)\n    update_constants_py(new_version)\n    update_version_file_txt(new_version)\n    \n    # Stage files for git\n    os.system(\"git add AUTOVERSION.py\")\n    os.system(\"git add config/constants.py\")\n    os.system(\"git add config/VERSION\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\n\u2713 Version bumped to {new_version}\")\n    print(\"  Files staged for commit\")\n    \n    return 0\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    sys.exit(main())\n", "sessionId": 327, "rowId": 3, "timestamp": 1784290602.3855765, "date": "2026-07-17", "name": "ReadFile"} -->
